### [1] [What Makes Linguistic Representations Good Models of High-Level Visual Perception in the Human Brain?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16214)
*Anna Bavaresco,Ina Klarić,Raquel Fernández,Marie-Francine Moens*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 用不同类型的图像说明文字（人类与多种机器生成）并用不同语言模型生成嵌入，评估其对高层视觉皮层脑响应与行为相似性判断的可预测性。机器字幕常优于人工字幕；面向语义任务的文本嵌入模型优于自回归LM；最佳预测出现在模型中层。结论：字幕内容与LM选择共同决定对脑与行为的拟合，字幕嵌入是研究高层视觉感知的有效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究显示：将图像描述输入语言模型得到的表征可预测人类在观看自然图像时的高层视觉脑响应，但不清楚驱动这种可预测性的关键因素是什么——是字幕本身的内容与风格，还是编码这些字幕的LM类型/层级。厘清这两类因素可推进脑-行为-模型对齐研究，并为选择更有效的表征方法提供原则。

Method: 对同一组图像，构造六类字幕（含人工与多种机器生成，覆盖长度、细节、风格等差异）；用五种LM将字幕表征化，覆盖自回归语言模型（下一个词预测）与面向语义任务微调的文本嵌入模型。评估：1）利用这些嵌入预测高层视觉脑区对图像的响应；2）测量与人类图像相似性判断的行为对齐；3）分析不同模型层的表征，定位预测性能随网络深度的变化。

Result: （1）多种机器字幕能显著预测脑响应并与行为对齐，常常超过传统使用的人类字幕。（2）跨字幕类型，文本嵌入模型稳定优于自回归LM；这一模式在行为相似性任务中复现。（3）分层分析显示，脑预测与行为对齐在中间层达到峰值，接近语法与语义结构被认为出现的阶段。

Conclusion: 图像字幕的内容选择与用于嵌入的LM类型共同影响对脑与行为数据的建模表现。优先使用面向语义的文本嵌入模型，并关注中间层表征，可提升对高层视觉表征的解释与预测。字幕嵌入为研究高层视觉感知与脑-行为对齐提供了有效、可控的工具。

Abstract: Image descriptions represented with language models (LMs) predict human brain responses to naturalistic images in high-level visual regions, but the factors driving this predictivity remain unclear. To investigate this, we systematically studied how images are described and which language models are used to embed those descriptions. For a common set of images, we considered six caption types -- including human-annotated and multiple machine-generated captions -- differing along several dimensions. Each caption was represented with five LMs, spanning autoregressive LMs trained to predict upcoming words and text embedders, i.e., LMs fine-tuned on semantic tasks requiring sentence/document-level representations. Machine-generated captions yielded significant brain predictivity and alignment, often surpassing human-annotated captions used in previous work. Across caption types, text embedders consistently outperformed autoregressive LMs, a pattern replicated when measuring behavioural alignment with image-similarity judgments. Analyses of caption representations from different model layers further revealed that both brain predictivity and behavioural alignment peak at intermediate network depth, shortly after a point thought to mark the emergence of syntactic and semantic structure. Altogether, our results demonstrate that both the content of image captions and the LM used to represent them influence brain- and behaviour-modelling performance, establishing caption embeddings as a useful tool for studying high-level visual perception.

</details>


### [2] [ForensicNet: Lightweight Attention-Enhanced MobileNetV2 for Automated Face Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16273)
*Savitha N J,Lata B T*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ForensicNet：以MobileNetV2为骨干并加入CBAM注意力、配合两阶段迁移学习与自适应解冻，实现在法证场景的人脸识别，精度92.4%，仅2.1 GFLOPs，适合实时应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 法证环境下人脸识别受姿态、光照、遮挡及标注数据稀缺影响，传统模型难以稳健识别且推理成本高，需要轻量且鲁棒的方案。

Method: 以MobileNetV2为主干，嵌入CBAM提升通道与空间注意力，强调判别性特征；采用两阶段迁移学习并自适应解冻层数以增强域适配、抑制过拟合；在LFW与SCFace等公开数据上训练/评估（约1.5万张、68类）。

Result: 相较AlexNet、ResNet-50、MobileNetV2基线，取得Accuracy 92.4%、Precision 90.8%、Recall 89.5%；单次推理仅2.1 GFLOPs，达到实时性。

Conclusion: 结合轻量骨干与注意力及稳健迁移策略，可在复杂法证条件下兼顾准确率与效率，适用于实时监控。

Abstract: In forensic environments, automated identification of perpetrators is difficult due to pose changes, changes in light, occlusion, and lack of labeled data. This paper presents ForensicNet, a lightweight deep learning framework for forensic face recognition that enhances attention. The suggested model combines the MobileNetV2 backbone with Convolutional Block Attention Modules (CBAM) to improve the learning of discriminative features while maintaining computational speed. A two-phase transfer learning strategy with adaptive layer unfreezing is used to improve domain adaptation and reduce overfitting. This study used publicly available datasets such as LFW and SCFace, with 15,000 facial images spanning 68 identity classes. The proposed model outperforms baseline architectures such as AlexNet, ResNet-50, and MobileNetV2, with an accuracy of 92.4%, a precision of 90.8%, and a recall of 89.5%. Additionally, the framework requires only 2.1 GFLOPs per inference, and hence can be used in real-time forensic surveillance applications.

</details>


### [3] [The JEPA Predictor: A Transferable Operator for Occluded Feature Completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16274)
*William Nguyen,Christopher Nguyen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该文发现并验证：将JEPA训练得到的“预测器”冻结后，通过一个小型线性映射即可移植到非JEPA编码器上，用于遮挡场景下的特征补全，显著提升部分可见分类性能，且增益随遮挡比例增加而单调上升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JEPA在训练时使用预测器辅助编码器，但下游通常丢弃预测器。作者提出：预测器本质是从可见上下文到被遮挡位置特征的学习算子，这正是部分视角分类所需。若能把该算子迁移到其他编码器上，可在不重训模型的前提下显著改进遮挡鲁棒性。

Method: 1) 在JEPA本身上，重用并冻结预测器，评估在高遮挡下对精度缺口的弥合；2) 将I-JEPA与V-JEPA v2的冻结预测器“加挂”到四个非JEPA编码器（CLIP、DINOv3、DINOv2、MAE），仅通过一个跨特征空间的单线性投影进行对接；该投影用ImageNet-1k的500张图闭式解拟合；3) 在ImageNet-9与Stanford Dogs上，跨三个遮挡比例K评估效果；并分析“线性桥”的固定代价与预测器带来的可变收益机制。

Result: - 在JEPA自身：保留冻结预测器显著缩小与最强判别式基线的差距，尤其在高遮挡下；- 迁移到非JEPA主干：所有“宿主-供体”组合上，性能提升相对各自的masked-encoder基线随K单调增加；- 典型结果：CLIP+I-JEPA预测器在ImageNet-9重遮挡下几乎找回被遮挡导致的大部分精度；在Stanford Dogs上由15.9%升至52.1%（+36个百分点）。

Conclusion: JEPA的冻结预测器可作为跨编码器家族的可移植“遮挡特征补全”算子。只需针对每个遮挡比例拟合一个匹配的线性投影与线性probe，无需重训编码器或预测器。其有效性在重遮挡下最强；在低遮挡且细粒度任务中，线性桥的固定代价可能超过补全收益，构成其失效边界。

Abstract: Joint-Embedding Predictive Architectures (JEPAs) train a predictor jointly with their encoder, but downstream deployment discards the predictor and reads features from the encoder alone. The predictor is, by construction, a learned operator from visible-context features to features at masked positions, the structure a partial-view classifier needs. We show that this operator is portable across encoder families. We first establish that, at heavy mask, retaining the frozen predictor on a JEPA encoder substantially closes the accuracy gap against the strongest non-JEPA discriminative baselines. We then bolt the frozen predictors of I-JEPA and V-JEPA 2 onto four non-JEPA hosts (CLIP, DINOv3, DINOv2, MAE) through a single linear projection between feature spaces, fit in closed form on 500 ImageNet-1k images. Across both ImageNet-9 and Stanford Dogs and across three mask fractions, the lift over each host's masked-encoder baseline grows monotonically with the mask fraction K in every host-donor pair. CLIP paired with the I-JEPA predictor recovers most of the accuracy that masking removed on ImageNet-9 at heavy occlusion, and lifts fine-grained Stanford Dogs from 15.9% to 52.1% (+36 pp). The mechanism is identifiable: the projection pays a fixed cost on visible patches and the predictor provides a growing benefit on masked patches; the benefit dominates the heavy-occlusion regime. At low K on fine-grained classification the projection cost exceeds the benefit, defining the boundary where the linear bridge breaks down. The frozen JEPA predictor functions as a portable operator for occluded feature completion across encoder families, requiring no retraining of either model while fitting matched linear probes per mask fraction.

</details>


### [4] [A Step Forward Towards Trustworthy Risk-Aware Facial Retrieval (RA-FR)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16279)
*Muhammad Emmad Siddiqui,Muhammad Rafi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出RA-FR风险感知人脸检索：在用户设定的风险α与置信1-δ下，自适应生成检索集合，确保包含真值；通过人脸恢复、鲁棒特征与保序校准三方面实现，在IMFDB上以约10张平均集合规模稳定满足5%风险目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实监控场景中分辨率低、模糊、光照不控导致域偏移，使得在基准上几乎完美的人脸识别在实务中出现漏检（假阴性），而漏掉目标在安防是不可接受的。需要一种能显式控制漏检风险并给出可审计保证的检索方法，而非固定Top-k。

Method: RA-FR包含三部分：1) 通过混合盲人脸恢复（InterLCM与DiffBIR耦合）降低随机不确定性；2) 用自监督DINOv1 ViT-B骨干+GGeM池化提取对恢复稳健的判别特征；3) 利用保形预测结合Hoeffding不等式，根据查询不确定性自适应校准检索集合大小，以满足用户设定的风险α与置信1-δ。

Result: 在IMFDB基准上，方法在保证目标5%风险水平的同时，平均检索集合约为10张，并能一致地满足风险约束。

Conclusion: 通过结合域特定恢复、鲁棒表示学习与具可证明保证的决策校准，RA-FR在非受限监控下实现既可靠又可审计的人脸检索，并提供开源代码以复现与应用。

Abstract: Facial image retrieval in unconstrained surveillance environments is a high-stakes challenge where missing a subject of interest -- a single false negative -- is simply not an option. Despite near-perfect performance on curated benchmarks, current recognition systems falter under real-world domain shifts such as low resolution, motion blur, and uncontrolled illumination (e.g., SCFace). Addressing this reliability gap, we propose Risk-Aware Facial Retrieval (RA-FR), a framework that moves beyond fixed Top-$k$ retrieval to adaptive set generation, guaranteeing ground truth inclusion within a user-specified risk level ($α$) and confidence level ($1 - δ$). Our approach integrates three core contributions: (1) reducing aleatoric uncertainty via a hybrid blind face restoration technique coupling Latent Consistency Models (InterLCM) and DiffBIR; (2) extracting discriminative, restoration-robust features via self-supervised DINOv1 ViT-B with GGeM pooling; and (3) employing conformal prediction with Hoeffding's inequality to dynamically calibrate retrieval set sizes based on query uncertainty. On the IMFDB benchmark, it consistently satisfies a 5% risk target with an average retrieval set size of approximately 10 images. By unifying domain-specific restoration, robust representation learning, and provable decision rules, RA-FR offers a pipeline that makes facial retrieval in surveillance both reliable and auditable. The code is available at: https://github.com/MuhammadEmmadSiddiqui/RA-FR.

</details>


### [5] [3D FaceShell: Attribute Transfer in 3D Face Avatars as a VLM Defense Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16280)
*Weston Bondurant,Srijan Das,Hieu Le,Stephanie Schuckers*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 3D FaceShell在3D人脸头像上加入可学习的高斯“外壳”，以跨视角一致地微扰渲染，使VLM对面部属性的语义推断被重定向，同时保持几何与身份不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共享的3D人脸头像在任意视角渲染后都可能被VLM推断出敏感属性，现有主要是2D防护，无法在保持身份的前提下对3D语义进行操控，存在隐私风险与缺口。

Method: 在原始3D头像外层添加可学习的Gaussian shell，进行多视角嵌入对齐训练，产生细微且空间分布的扰动；优化目标是跨视角一致地影响黑箱VLM的属性推断，同时约束几何保真、感知相似度与身份一致性。

Result: 在名人重建头像与多种黑箱VLM上，显著提高了属性注入与属性不匹配率，同时保持高感知相似度与身份一致性，效果跨视角稳定且扰动不显眼。

Conclusion: 可以在不破坏人类可识别外观的情况下，稳定操控VLM对3D人脸的语义解读，为3D头像的隐私保护与语义可控提供新方向。

Abstract: Photorealistic 3D face avatars are increasingly deployed as reusable digital assets across applications such as telepresence, animation, and personalized media. At the same time, vision-language models (VLMs) can infer sensitive attributes from rendered images with open-ended semantic reasoning without any fine-tuning. This creates a new privacy challenge: once a 3D face avatar is shared, any of its renderings can be analyzed to extract high-level facial attributes. Existing defenses largely operate in 2D image space and do not address identity-preserving semantic manipulation of 3D facial representations. We propose 3D FaceShell, a framework for steering VLM interpretations of faces rendered from 3D models while preserving geometric fidelity and facial identity. 3D FaceShell augments the original 3D representation with a learnable Gaussian shell that produces subtle, spatially distributed perturbations optimized through multi-view embedding alignment. The perturbations are designed to be visually inconspicuous yet sufficient to redirect VLM-based attribute inference in a view-consistent manner. Extensive experiments on reconstructed celebrity face avatars and multiple black-box VLMs demonstrate that 3D FaceShell significantly increases attribute injection and mismatch rates while maintaining high perceptual similarity and identity consistency. Our results show that it is possible to manipulate VLM-level semantic interpretation of 3D faces without compromising their human-recognizable appearance.

</details>


### [6] [Moving Like a Human: Ego-Motion-Normalized Temporal Signatures for Real-Time Aerial Person Tracking on Milliwatt-Class Hardware](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16282)
*Akbar Anbar Jafari,Cagri Ozcinar,Gholamreza Anbarjafari*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EMTS-Det 提出在资源受限无人机上进行“跟随我”人形跟踪的端侧方案：用解析的自运动估计与残差运动通道作为输入，配合极小网络完成检测与跟踪验证，在低像素目标和极小算力下显著优于大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机随行场景中，目标人在画面中仅有10–60像素，单帧外观特征与杂波难以区分；同时机载算力仅有少量int8 GFLOP/s，无法承载大型时序网络。作者认为关键证据是时间域运动信息，应通过解析的自运动对齐与残差运动显式编码到输入，而非依赖重型的学习式时序模块。

Method: 构建五阶段流水线：1) 估计机体自运动；2) 将每帧转换为经自运动归一化的残差运动通道；3) 用仅2.2万参数、7.6 MFLOP的轻量检测器预测人中心；4) 在稳定坐标系用卡尔曼滤波跟踪锁定目标；5) 用1D卷积对运动序列做人体运动验证（ROC AUC=0.941）。训练采用合成运动课程学习，运动通道由部署的自运动代码生成；进行多种消融与量化校准策略。

Result: 在VisDrone-DET保留集上，若仅用亮度通道AP25从0.415降至0.051；同样数据下，YOLOv8n虽算力高1100倍也崩至0.051。部署的int8检测器域内AP25=0.694，在该分割上为0.444。时间偏移模块反而降准，最终检测器无状态。记录到静默的int8校准失败；采用min-max并传播缓存的校准与float结果相差≤0.008 AP。Raspberry Pi Zero 2W上整管线31.85 FPS，AP25=0.462、召回0.714（1000段真实UAV视频）；对比YOLOv8n仅1.95 FPS、AP25=0.172。实地57秒序列中1.3 s自动锁定，97.9%锁定召回，9次遮挡均恢复且零误重锁。

Conclusion: 将时间信息显式注入输入（经自运动补偿的残差运动）比学习式时序模块更有效且更省算，能在极低算力平台稳定实现低像素目标的跟踪检测。轻量化、无状态检测+传统跟踪与运动验证的组合，在真实无人机场景中显著优于大模型；正确的int8校准对端侧性能至关重要。

Abstract: Follow-me person tracking must run on the drone itself, where affordable companion computers offer only a few effective int8 GFLOP/s. At typical follow distances a person spans 10-60 pixels, indistinguishable from clutter and beyond the reach of single-frame appearance detectors. The missing evidence is temporal and belongs in the input representation, computed analytically, rather than in learned temporal machinery. EMTS-Det is a five-stage system that estimates ego-motion, converts each frame into ego-motion-normalized residual-motion channels, detects person centers with a 22k-parameter, 7.6-MFLOP network, tracks a locked target with a Kalman filter in stabilized coordinates, and verifies tracks with a 1-D convolutional classifier of human motion (ROC AUC 0.941). Training uses a synthetic-motion curriculum with motion channels generated by the deployed ego-motion code. Multi-seed ablations locate the value in generalization: on held-out VisDrone-DET a luminance-only variant collapses to 0.051 AP25 versus 0.415, as does YOLOv8n fine-tuned identically despite 1,100 times the compute, while the deployed int8 detector reaches 0.694 AP25 in-domain and 0.444 on this split. Temporal-shift modules lower accuracy, so the deployed detector is stateless. Silent int8 calibration failures are documented; min-max calibration with propagated caches matches float within 0.008 AP. On a Raspberry Pi Zero 2W the pipeline runs at 31.85 FPS with 0.462 AP25 and 0.714 recall over 1,000 real-world UAV videos, versus 1.95 FPS and 0.172 AP25 for YOLOv8n. A 57-second field sequence shows auto-lock at 1.3 s, 97.9% lock recall, and recovery from all nine occlusions with zero false re-locks.

</details>


### [7] [GenSyn10: A Multi-Generative AI Dataset For Benchmarking Image Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16283)
*Md Faraz Kabir Khan,Saeed Anwar,Ghulam Mubashar Hassan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GenSyn10：与CIFAR-10对齐的6万张合成图像数据集，用多种SOTA生成器统一协议生成，用于评测与提升AI生成图像检测的跨生成器泛化。基准显示：已见生成器上接近满分，但对未见生成器仍显著下降，凸显OOD难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有合成内容检测器在训练见过的生成器上表现好，但对未见生成器显著退化；缺乏一个多架构、可控、与常用视觉基准对齐的数据集来系统研究跨生成器与OOD泛化。

Method: 构建GenSyn10：对齐CIFAR-10（10类、32×32、50k/10k），使用三种架构各异的SOTA生成模型（FLUX.2-dev、HunyuanImage-3.0、Qwen-Image-2512）在标准化模板提示与下采样协议下生成。设计四阶段评测：真实数据基线、零样本迁移、微调、保留性（retention）。评测17个图像分类模型在多生成器与未见生成器情境下的表现。

Result: 尽管存在域差距，用CIFAR-10训练的模型在GenSyn10上零样本最高达96.86%，微调后至99.88%。二分类（真vs合成）中，微调后在已见生成器上97–99.9%准确率，但在未见生成器上降至79–96%，显示跨生成器泛化仍有限。

Conclusion: GenSyn10提供一个受控、与CIFAR-10兼容的基准，用于研究合成图像检测的鲁棒性、域适配与跨生成器泛化；当前方法对未知生成器仍存在明显性能缺口，亟需改进OOD泛化策略。

Abstract: The rapid advancement of generative AI has outpaced our ability to reliably detect its outputs, particularly when detectors encounter generators they have not seen before. We introduce GenSyn10, a CIFAR-10-aligned synthetic image dataset of 60,000 images (10 classes, 32$\times$32, 50k/10k split) generated using three architecturally diverse state-of-the-art models: FLUX.2-dev (Rectified Flow Transformer), HunyuanImage-3.0 (MoE Transformer), and Qwen-Image-2512 (Multimodal Diffusion Transformer), to advance research in AI-generated image detection. A central challenge in this domain is that detectors perform well on known generators but degrade on unseen ones. GenSyn10 addresses this limitation by curating data from multiple contemporary architectures under a standardized generation protocol, enabling controlled and systematic evaluation of out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization to novel generators. Images are generated using a template-based prompt engine and downsampled to ensure consistency. We evaluate 17 image classification models under a four-stage protocol: real-data baseline, zero-shot transfer, fine-tuning, and retention. Despite a measurable domain gap, CIFAR-10-trained models achieve up to 96.86\% zero-shot accuracy on GenSyn10, increasing to 99.88\% after fine-tuning. In binary real-vs-synthetic classification, fine-tuned models achieve 97-99.9\% accuracy on seen generators but drop to 79-96\% on images from an unseen generator, highlighting persistent limitations in OOD generalization. These results establish GenSyn10 as a controlled benchmark for studying synthetic image detection beyond single-generator settings, supporting research on robustness, domain adaptation, and cross-generator generalization.

</details>

### [9] [A Shared Latent for Partially-Labeled Multi-Task Facial Affect Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16285)
*Hong Hai Nguyen,Sy Phan Van,Soo-Hyung Kim,Van-Thong Huynh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出一种在部分标注场景下联合学习面部情感多任务（价-唤醒、离散表情、动作单元）的变分共享潜变量方法，在s-Aff-Wild2上无需源数据预训练，即便仅37%帧具备全标注、类别极度不均衡，也能显著提升表达识别宏F1，并与严格对照实验表明增益来自表示层面的跨任务耦合，而非损失权重技巧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实“野外”人脸情感数据对多任务标注稀疏且不均衡，常见做法要么屏蔽缺失标签要么用伪标注，导致各任务间潜在共享信息无法被充分利用。作者希望在不依赖外部预训练和外部数据的限制下，系统性地利用跨任务信号，缓解少数类与缺失标注带来的性能瓶颈，并用严谨对照验证增益来源。

Method: 将部分标注的多任务学习表述为对共享情感潜变量的边缘化：采用单一变分瓶颈作为编码器/潜变量，三个任务（VA、离散表情、AU）各自作为解码器；对缺失标签不再简单mask，而是把“被mask的目标”转化为证据下界（ELBO）中的重构项。使用s-Aff-Wild2，在不允许源数据预训练的设定下，基于单一骨干网络分析跨任务耦合的作用；进一步加入第二个、误差去相关的骨干以突破AU性能上限。全程配套匹配对照（negative controls）以识别增益机制。

Result: 在s-Aff-Wild2上：单骨干下，离散表情宏F1从专用单任务模型的0.403提升到0.446，超过“仅mask缺失标签”的基线；加入第二个误差去相关的骨干后，动作单元性能突破此前需外部AU数据也难以越过的上限；价-唤醒保持在统计噪声范围内波动。所有提升均被匹配的负向对照约束，显示改进源于表示学习而非损失塑形。综合多任务得分验证集达到1.679。对AffectNet与RAF-DB的迁移仅呈现小幅、依赖设置的增益，作为探索性结果。

Conclusion: 基于共享变分潜变量的部分标注多任务框架能有效利用跨任务信号，缓解类别不平衡与标注缺失带来的瓶颈，尤其提升表情与动作单元任务；收益主要来自更好的共享表示而非损失工程。方法在严格无预训练设定与负向对照下成立，但跨数据集的迁移收益有限，需进一步研究泛化与任务解耦/耦合策略。

Abstract: Facial affect in the wild is naturally multi-task: valence-arousal, discrete expressions, and facial action units describe the same face. Yet real corpora annotate these tasks only partially and unevenly, so most systems mask the missing labels or impute pseudo-labels and forgo the cross-task signal. We instead cast partially-labeled multi-task learning as marginalization over a shared affect latent: one variational bottleneck mediates all three task decoders, so a frame annotated for one task shapes the representation the others use, and the masked objective reappears as the reconstruction term of an evidence lower bound. On s-Aff-Wild2, where only 37% of frames carry all three labels, the classes are severely imbalanced, and pretraining on the source data is disallowed, we isolate where this coupling acts. On a single backbone it lifts expression macro-F1 from 0.403 for a dedicated specialist to 0.446, which the masked-loss model does not reach; a second, near-peer backbone with decorrelated errors then breaks an action-unit ceiling that external action-unit data could not, while valence-arousal stays within noise. Every gain is disciplined by a matched-control negative; together these controls indicate that the rare-class failure is representational, not a matter of loss shaping. As each task's source is chosen on the evaluation split, we report the assembled result, a combined multi-task score of 1.679 on validation, as an in-sample endpoint and rest our conclusions on the controlled comparisons; a small, regime-dependent transfer of the expression advantage to AffectNet and RAF-DB is presented as exploratory rather than conclusive.

### [10] [Depth Estimators Are Implicit Neural Fields for 3D Scene Geometry Inpainting and Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16286)
*Yingzhao Jian,Zihao Lin,Hehe Fan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Neural Depth Field（NDF），在测试时统一优化以修复3D场景几何并保证与观测一致，跨多域达到SOTA：跨视角不一致降63.3%，补全精度升23.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实场景的3D几何常有缺失；现有用深度估计器补洞的方法要么与已观测几何不一致，要么在分布外数据上不可靠。需要一种既能适应目标域又能保持与观测一致的方案。

Method: 将深度估计器视为场景级隐式场：在测试时通过学习观测到的深度数据进行适应（估计器属性），同时作为隐式场拟合现有几何以保证一致性（隐式场属性）。采用单次测试时优化（test-time optimization）统一解决域适应与一致性问题，输出全局一致、可补全的深度/几何。

Result: 在多种场景（室内扫描、卫星影像等）上产生高保真、全局一致的几何：跨视角不一致性降低63.3%，补全（inpainting）精度提升23.1%，达到当前最优表现。

Conclusion: 将深度估计与隐式场统一为NDF，通过测试时优化实现跨域适应与几何一致性，显著提升3D场景几何补全质量与稳定性，并具有广泛适用性；代码已开源。

Abstract: The 3D geometry of real-world scene data is often incomplete. Mainstream methods use depth estimators to inpaint missing structure. However, their prediction results can be inconsistent with observed geometry, or unreliable on out-of-distribution data. To solve these problems, we propose Neural Depth Field (NDF). Our key insight is that a depth estimator can also be a scene-level implicit field. As an estimator, it adapts to the target domain by learning observed depth data. As an implicit field, it fits the existing geometry to maintain consistency. Under this view, NDF addresses both problems through a single test-time optimization. Experiments show that NDF produces high-fidelity and globally consistent geometry across diverse scene data, ranging from indoor scans to satellite imagery. It reduces cross-view inconsistency by 63.3\% and improves inpainting accuracy by 23.1\%, achieving state-of-the-art performance in 3D scene geometry inpainting. The code is available at: https://github.com/Shadow-Dream/Neural-Depth-Field.

### [11] [Identity-Consistent Expression Fields: A Disentangled Neural Radiance Field Framework for Few-Shot Facial Expression Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16287)
*Minh Tran*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ICEF提出在少样本人脸动态NeRF中显式分离身份辐射场与表情形变，并通过身份保持正则与置信加权条件扭曲，提升远离训练表情时的身份一致性与渲染质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有少样本动态NeRF通常以单一特征体积在目标表情条件下整体扭曲，面对超出少样本分布的表情会导致身份相关外观细节（皮肤纹理、细微几何）漂移与伪影，缺乏对身份与表情因素的解耦与约束。

Method: 1) 构建Identity-Consistent Expression Fields：将静态、身份特定的辐射分量与动态、由表情参数驱动的形变分量显式解耦；2) 身份保持正则：约束形变网络仅在与表情相关的区域发生变化，尽量不改动规范姿态下的身份外观；3) 置信加权的条件特征扭曲：对距离少样本表情参数较远的目标表情降低扭曲强度，抑制外推时的错误变形与伪影；4) 提供与现有少样本动态NeRF、静态3D人脸生成、解耦式辐射场方法的关系分析与实现细节。

Result: 在评测协议下（覆盖不同表情参数外推距离），ICEF在新表情渲染质量与身份一致性指标上均优于现有少样本动态NeRF方法，特别是在大幅外推场景中显著减少身份细节漂移与伪影。

Conclusion: 显式解耦身份辐射与表情形变，并以身份保持正则与置信加权扭曲进行约束，是在少样本条件下实现稳健新表情合成和身份一致性的有效途径；该框架为动态人脸NeRF的少样本外推提供了更可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Neural Radiance Fields (NeRF) have enabled photorealistic novel-view synthesis of 3D scenes and, in the facial domain, have been extended to reconstruct and animate 3D face models from a small number of images. However, existing few-shot dynamic NeRF methods for facial expression editing typically warp a single learned feature volume conditioned on target expression parameters, which can cause identity-specific appearance details (skin texture, fine geometric structure) to drift when the model is driven toward expressions far from those seen in the few-shot input set. We propose Identity-Consistent Expression Fields (ICEF), a framework that explicitly disentangles a static, identity-specific radiance component from a dynamic, expression-conditioned deformation component, and introduces an identity preservation regularizer that constrains the deformation network to modify only expression-relevant regions while leaving identity-specific canonical appearance untouched. ICEF further incorporates a confidence-weighted conditional feature warping step that down-weights unreliable warps for target expressions that are far, in parameter space, from the observed few-shot inputs, mitigating artifacts observed in prior few-shot dynamic NeRF methods when extrapolating to novel expressions. We relate ICEF to prior few-shot dynamic NeRF, static 3D-aware face generation, and disentangled face-editing radiance field methods, and describe an evaluation protocol measuring both novel-expression rendering quality and, specifically, identity-consistency metrics across a range of expression-parameter extrapolation distances.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实制造中缺陷样本稀少且标注昂贵，导致点云深度学习检测在数据量、类别不平衡和罕见缺陷识别上受限；需要能同时控制零件设计与缺陷形态的合成数据来缓解。

Method: 用参数化CAD生成齿轮几何，尺寸参数在±0.0254 mm范围扰动；缺陷参数按形态分布采样；为每个网格用Open3D均匀采样10万点生成点云，输出为N×3坐标文本；提供元数据标签（设计、质量类别）。共构建12种设计、4种质量类别，合计24,000对网格与点云。

Result: 得到一个可公开获取的合成数据集MFGNet-Gear，规模化、类别均衡、全标注，适配设计分类、几何缺陷检测、表征学习与基准评测等任务。

Abstract: Quality control in smart manufacturing increasingly relies on data-driven methods, particularly deep learning, to automate the inspection of manufactured parts. However, deep learning methods for point-cloud-based inspection require large volumes of labeled data covering part designs and defect types, which are costly and time-consuming to obtain. Moreover, defective parts are intrinsically rare in mass production, and the resulting class imbalance can degrade model performance and make rare defect types difficult to detect. Synthetic data generation (SDG) offers a promising approach to address these challenges by producing large, balanced, and fully annotated datasets. Yet, applying SDG to precision components requires representing part geometry and defect morphology parametrically, so that design and quality can be co-varied. This article describes MFGNet-Gear, a publicly available synthetic 3D dataset comprising 24,000 paired polygon meshes and point clouds across 12 gear designs and 4 quality classes, with 500 instances per design-quality combination. Gear geometries are generated with parametric computer-aided design software, with dimensional parameters perturbed by $\pm$0.0254 mm and defect parameters sampled from distributions representing defect morphologies. For each mesh, 100,000 points are uniformly sampled using Open3D and stored as N $\times$ 3 coordinate text files. Metadata labels identify the gear design and quality class, supporting part design classification, geometric defect detection, representation learning, and dataset benchmarking. MFGNet-Gear provides an open-source dataset for deep learning-based 3D metrology, with a reproducible generation pipeline extensible to additional part designs.

### [13] [Strength-Parity Ensembling with Parameter-Isolated Experts for Multi-Task Affect Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16290)
*Hong Hai Nguyen,Van Thong Huynh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对ABAW挑战多任务赛道（情感价-唤醒、表情识别、动作单元检测），提出“实力均衡+去相关”的集成准则，并用参数子空间隔离构建去相关且性能相近的专家，从而在不允许Aff-Wild2预训练的规则下显著提升验证分数至1.7259。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有领先方案依赖大型集成，但很少阐明应向强集成中加入哪些成员。多任务、长尾与缺失标签场景下，盲目扩增常无效，因为成员间高度相关、且个体精度差距过大。需要一个可操作的原则来选择/构造能真正降低误差的新增模型。

Method: 1) 共享情感潜变量：两条受情感监督的骨干共享一个潜在表征，对缺失标签进行边缘化以联合学习价-唤醒、8类表情、12类AU。2) 提出“实力均衡（near-peer）+去相关（decorrelated）”的集成准则：新增成员需同时与现有成员低相关、且个体精度接近。3) 诊断：在单一骨干上通过不同随机种子或微调课程，预测相关性仍收敛至0.98，难以提供多样性。4) 参数隔离：将每个专家的适配限制在共享骨干的不相交低秩子空间（低秩适配/子空间路由），使专家间相关性降至0.91且维持近似精度；其中AffectNet适配专家最强。5) 进一步技巧：对AU做校准；将共享潜变量头的价-唤醒支路作为额外近似同侪加入集成。

Result: 在验证集上总体评分由基线ConvNeXt+MixAugment的0.45提升至1.6949；加入AU校准并把价-唤醒支路作为近似同侪后，最佳配置达1.7259。专家间相关性由0.98降至0.91，同时保持个体性能相近。

Conclusion: 要想在强集成上继续降错，新增模型必须既去相关又与现有成员实力相当。常规重启/课程变化难以产生足够多样性；通过参数子空间隔离可系统性地产生近似同侪且低相关的专家，从而在多任务、长尾、缺失标签且受限预训练的场景下实现显著增益。

Abstract: Leading entries on the multi-task track of the 11th ABAW challenge rely on heavy ensembling, yet which member is worth adding to an already strong ensemble is rarely made explicit. We study this question for joint valence-arousal estimation, 8-way expression recognition, and 12-way action-unit detection from a single unconstrained face, under partial, long-tailed labels and a rule that forbids pretraining on Aff-Wild2. Building on a shared affect-latent that marginalizes the missing labels across two affect-supervised backbones, we propose a strength-parity rule: an added member lowers the ensemble error only when it is both decorrelated from the current members and a near-peer of them in individual accuracy. The rule exposes a concrete obstacle, as on a single backbone re-seeding and even distinct fine-tuning curricula re-converge to a prediction correlation of 0.98 and add no diversity. Parameter-isolation removes it: confining each adaptation to a disjoint low-rank subspace of a shared backbone yields experts that stay decorrelated at 0.91 while remaining near-peers, the strongest of them an AffectNet-adapted expert. The resulting system raises the overall validation score to 1.6949, against the organizers ConvNeXt-with-MixAugment baseline of 0.45; with per-AU calibration and by pooling the shared-latent heads valence-arousal byproduct as a further near-peer, the strongest configuration reaches 1.7259.

</details>


### [14] [Beyond Target Scores: Measuring Off-Target Drift in Diffusion-Based Medical Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16291)
*Todd Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CIB-Med-1基准，用轨迹级（随编辑强度变化的序列）评估胸片中胸腔积液的“受控生物标志物编辑”，同时量化目标进展、逆转率与14类临床扰动轴上的离靶语义漂移；发现扩散编辑存在“奖励黑客”，并给出受约束引导方法，在几乎保持目标趋势的同时显著降低离靶漂移，并得到盲法人工验证支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医学影像编辑多以目标评分是否上升评估，但临床中目标征象与合并症、采集效应、选择偏倚高度纠缠，模型可能通过改动相关但非目标的征象来“看似达标”。需要一个能分离目标与离靶变化、以轨迹控制为核心的新评估框架。

Method: 构建CIB-Med-1：聚焦胸片中胸腔积液的定向编辑，沿编辑轨迹评估三类指标——校准的目标进展、逆转率、以及在14条临床动机的干扰轴（实变、慢性征象、伪影等）上的离靶语义漂移；揭示现有扩散编辑的奖励黑客；提出“受约束的扩散引导”基线，在优化目标进展的同时对离靶变化设定上界。进行持出胸片与盲法人工（放射科住培医师）验证，并与Pix2Pix等方法比较。

Result: 与无约束引导相比，受约束编辑保持相近的目标趋势相关（ρ_trend=0.88 vs 0.90），将中位离靶漂移由0.46降至0.20，90分位由0.98降至0.33；离靶漂移大小与实证的目标-非目标关联一致，表明语义不稳定具结构性；盲评中与预期进展排序的一致性更强（τ=0.61），优于Pix2Pix（0.29）。

Conclusion: 医学影像编辑的评估应转向“轨迹级语义控制”而非“终点分数最大化”。CIB-Med-1揭示并量化扩散编辑的奖励黑客，并给出能显著抑制离靶漂移的受约束引导基线，为更稳健、可控的临床影像编辑评估与方法提供路径。

Abstract: Diffusion models can now edit medical images in visually plausible ways, but the standard evaluation question is too narrow: did the target score increase? In clinical imaging, target findings are entangled with co-morbidities, acquisition effects, and selection bias, so a model can appear successful by changing correlated non-target findings rather than isolating the intended pathology. We introduce CIB-Med-1, a trajectory-level benchmark for controlled biomarker editing in chest radiography. CIB-Med-1 evaluates directional pleural effusion editing through calibrated target progression, inversion rate, and off-target semantic drift over 14 clinically motivated nuisance axes. The benchmark exposes a reward-hacking failure mode in which diffusion editors increase effusion scores while simultaneously altering parenchymal, cardiomediastinal, pleural, chronic, or artifact-related findings. We further present a constrained diffusion guidance baseline that optimizes target progression subject to bounded off-target change. Across held-out radiographs, the constrained editor preserves target progression ($ρ_{\mathrm{trend}}=0.88$ vs. $0.90$ for unconstrained guidance) while reducing median off-target drift from $0.46$ to $0.20$ and 90th-percentile drift from $0.98$ to $0.33$. Drift magnitude tracks empirical target--off-target association, supporting the view that semantic instability is structured rather than incidental. A blinded human validation probe with radiology trainees further shows stronger agreement with intended progression orderings ($τ=0.61$ vs.\ $0.29$ for Pix2Pix). These results argue that medical image editing should be evaluated as trajectory-level semantic control, not as endpoint score maximization.

</details>


### [15] [It Depends on the Dataset: When a Brain-Encoding Model's Predicted Responses Beat Their Visual Backbone for Video Memorability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16292)
*Carson Rodrigues*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 利用TRIBE v2等脑编码基础模型生成的“无扫描仪”预测皮层响应，用于短视频可记忆性预测；在VideoMem数据集上胜过视觉骨干，在Memento10k上则相反，显示数据集特异的增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验“预测脑表征”是否为下游人类行为任务（记忆性预测）提供独立且有用的信息，相较于仅用视觉自监督骨干特征。

Method: 将每个视频投影到TRIBE v2预测的皮层响应空间；以ridge回归预测短期记忆性。对照：使用同一模型的V-JEPA2视觉骨干特征（投影前）。进行数据内和跨数据集评测、bootstrap置信区间、大小匹配、PCA-then-ridge、压缩/强正则骨干、以及迁移调优骨干的对比。部分相关与置换检验定位信号脑区。

Result: Memento10k内：骨干优于脑投影（Spearman 0.594 vs 0.544）。VideoMem内：脑投影优于骨干（0.415 vs 0.368，Δ+0.047，95% CI [+0.009,+0.088]）。两者差异均显著且方向相反。跨数据：训Memento10k测VideoMem脑投影更好（+0.076）；反向迁移骨干劣化（-0.311）。VideoMem上的优势非样本量或压缩效应造成；脑投影也优于迁移调优骨干（+0.053）。存在与视觉骨干正交的成分（部分Spearman 0.19，p=2.5e-4），定位于腹侧枕颞皮层。

Conclusion: 预测脑表征在视频记忆性上提供小但真实、且数据集特异的增益；不是通用先验，而是与数据域相关的表示。公开代码与预测响应数组（不含原视频与分数）。

Abstract: Brain-encoding foundation models predict fMRI responses to video, audio, and text well enough to win the Algonauts 2025 challenge. We ask whether their predicted responses, obtained with no scanner, are a useful feature lens for a downstream human-behavior task: forecasting the memorability of short videos. We project each clip into TRIBE v2's predicted cortical space and forecast short-term memorability with ridge regression, against a matched control: the model's own V-JEPA2 visual backbone taken before the brain projection. The answer is dataset-dependent, and cleanly so. Within Memento10k the backbone wins (Spearman 0.594 vs 0.544 for the brain projection); within VideoMem the brain projection wins (0.415 vs 0.368, delta +0.047, 95% CI [+0.009, +0.088]). Both within-dataset gaps have bootstrap intervals excluding zero, in opposite directions. Cross-dataset transfer inherits the split: trained on Memento10k and tested on VideoMem the brain projection beats the backbone (+0.076), while the reverse loses heavily (-0.311). Each representation transfers best onto the dataset it already fits better. The VideoMem advantage is not a sample-size artifact (it survives matched training size and a PCA-then-ridge pipeline) and not mere compression of the backbone (a compressed or heavily regularized backbone tops out below the brain projection, which also beats a transfer-tuned backbone, +0.053). So predicted-brain features carry a small but real memorability signal the backbone misses on one dataset and not the other: not a domain-general prior, but a dataset-specific representation. A vision-orthogonal component (partial Spearman 0.19, permutation p=2.5e-4) localizes to ventral occipito-temporal cortex. Code and predicted-response arrays are released; source videos and scores are not redistributed.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小规模医疗图像分类常伴随噪声标签，深度网络易过拟合噪声；QNN在小数据下有潜力，但其“天然平滑性”既可正则化也会掩盖高置信样本，难以进行噪声转移矩阵估计。亟需一种既适配QNN特性又能稳健估计/更新噪声转移的框架。

Method: 将模型预测分布的熵下降过程建模为上超鞅，利用其单调性选择稳定的转移矩阵细化步骤，形成无锚点的动态标签转移更新与损失校正；并给出该细化过程收敛至稳态的理论分析。

Conclusion: 通过上超鞅建模实现的无锚点转移矩阵细化，可缓解QNN天然平滑性带来的高置信样本稀缺问题，提供可收敛、稳健的噪声标签学习方案，适用于小样本医疗图像分类并优于现有基线。

Abstract: Noisy-label learning in small-scale medical image classification is challenging and hinders the superiority of deep neural networks. Recent studies suggest that quantum neural networks (QNNs) have shown potential in limited-data regimes, yet their use for noisy-label learning remains under-explored. A key obstacle is QNNs' intrinsic "natural smoothness", which may regularize training but also obscure high-confidence samples needed for noise-transition estimation. We propose Supermartingale-based Label Transition (SLT), an anchor-free loss correction framework for robust QNN-based medical image classification under noisy labels. SLT models entropy reduction in predictive distributions as a supermartingale and uses its monotonic behavior to identify stable transition-matrix refinement steps. This enables dynamic transition updates while reducing noise-driven oscillations during QNN training. We further provide a convergence analysis showing that the proposed transition-refinement process reaches a steady state. Experiments on multiple public small-scale medical image datasets demonstrate that SLT consistently improves QNN-based classification and stably outperforms classic noise-label learning baselines under synthetic and real-world label noise.

### [17] [A${}^2$BM: Alignment-Aware Bridge Matching for Image-to-Image Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16294)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实应用中配对图像常因不同采集条件产生错位与弱对齐，现有桥匹配/流匹配与扩散式方法默认完美对齐，等权对待配对，容易把错位当作语义，导致译图伪影与语义漂移。

Method: 在桥匹配框架中引入对齐分数：训练时以对齐分数加权/条件化学习，让模型区分真实语义对应与错位伪影；推理时把对齐分数作为控制变量调节翻译保真度，给定较高分数可得到更强对齐、较低分数允许更自由的变化。

Result: 在合成实验与真实任务（跨传感器超分、像素空间的无监督域自适应）上，相比强基线（GAN、扩散、薛定谔桥）均取得更高的翻译保真度与稳定性。

Conclusion: 对齐条件作为训练与推理的显式信号，可系统缓解弱对齐数据带来的配对翻译误差；A^2BM为弱对齐场景提供了原则化且可控的解决方案。

Abstract: Paired image-to-image translation underpins a wide range of computer vision tasks, including image editing, sensor translation, and domain adaptation. Bridge matching and flow matching have recently emerged as powerful frameworks, extending diffusion models to arbitrary source and target distributions. However, their standard formulations assume perfectly aligned training pairs, treating all source-target correspondences as equally reliable. In practice, real-world applications often involve weakly aligned pairs due to changes of acquisition conditions, including e.g. asynchronous captures, different illuminations, or misregistration. In this work, we introduce Alignment-Aware Bridge Matching (A${}^2$BM), a bridge matching method that leverages image pairs alignment during training. By incorporating alignment scores, the model learns to disentangle true semantic correspondences from misalignment artifacts. At inference time, we use the alignment score as a control variable over translation fidelity, with strongly aligned outputs obtained when prompting the model with the highest alignment score. We validate A${}^2$BM on both controlled synthetic experiments and on challenging real-world tasks, including cross-sensor super-resolution and pixel-space unsupervised domain adaptation. In all settings, A${}^2$BM consistently improves translation fidelity over strong GAN-, diffusion-, and Schr{ö}dinger bridge-based baselines, establishing alignment conditioning as a principled solution for image translation models with weakly aligned data.

### [18] [Emergent Hierarchical Monosemantic Neurons from the Group-Contrastive Forward-Forward Algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16295)
*Yiming Tang,Qinglin Qi,Zhaoqian Yao,Harshvardhan Saini,Dianbo Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种生物启发的前向前向训练算法GCFF，通过类内对比与类特定路由在结构上诱导单义神经元，克服SDL/稀疏自编码器对线性可分与可辨识性假设的局限，并在CLIP与从零训练上均表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有稀疏字典学习（如稀疏自编码器）在可解释性上面临：目标不可辨识；强依赖线性表示假设；越来越多证据表明概念是非线性编码、无法用单一方向表示。受生物视觉系统的层级与局部学习启发，作者探索无需全局误差信号、能产生选择性强（单义）神经元的替代路径。

Method: 提出Group-Contrastive Forward-Forward（GCFF）：在Forward-Forward框架中引入（1）类特定路由（group-specific routing）以在结构上分解表示空间；（2）类内对比目标以在同类样本间形成判别特征；叠加多层非线性到被研究表示之上，使神经元可表征非线性概念；无需稀疏约束与抽象层级监督。

Result: 在CLIP特征上，单个GCFF模块即可恢复随深度逐层抽象的单义神经元，能识别与前景无关的环境属性等高层概念。GCFF还能从头训练网络，在多种图像分类基准上取得Forward-Forward方法的SOTA性能。

Conclusion: 通过结构性约束与生物可行的前向学习，GCFF在不依赖稀疏性和线性假设下实现单义表示，并兼具良好任务性能，提供了超越SDL范式的可解释性与训练新路径。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability has made significant strides in understanding neural network representations, with sparse dictionary learning (SDL) methods, most prominently sparse autoencoders, as a central paradigm. However, recent work has reported several limitations of this paradigm: SDL objectives are non-identifiable; SDL methods rely heavily on the Linear Representation Hypothesis; and a growing body of evidence points to concepts that are encoded non-linearly and are therefore not expressible as any single direction. We hypothesise that a different route to monosemanticity is available. Biological visual systems exhibit highly selective neurons organised into hierarchies of increasing abstraction, and this organisation emerges from local, layer-wise learning rules rather than from a global error signal; we therefore ask whether a biologically plausible learning algorithm will likewise yield monosemantic neurons. To test this, we propose Group-Contrastive Forward-Forward (GCFF), a forward-forward training algorithm that combines class-specific routing with within-class contrastive objectives, reaching monosemanticity through architectural constraints rather than sparsity. Because GCFF attaches multiple non-linear layers to the representation under study, its neurons can therefore capture the non-linear concepts. On CLIP representations, a single trained GCFF module recovers monosemantic neurons whose abstraction increases progressively with depth, reaching environmental properties that hold independently of an image's foreground, without any sparsity constraint or supervision of abstraction level. We further demonstrate that GCFF can train networks from scratch, achieving state-of-the-art performance among forward-forward algorithms on various image classification benchmarks.

### [19] [Rethinking Feature Reliance Evaluation with Semantically Matched Suppression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16298)
*Ning Jiang,Tianyi Luo,Zhengyong Huang,Yao Sui*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文通过语义匹配的特征抑制框架，公平比较形状与纹理对模型识别的贡献，发现CNN在纹理被抑制时性能降幅更大，而ViT在两类抑制下更稳健，并与大脑表征更一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往“线索冲突”(cue-conflict)实验多在形状与纹理相矛盾的合成情境下评估偏好，不能反映模型在自然识别中的真实特征依赖；同时，不同抑制方法造成的类别可分性损伤不一致，导致对“性能下降=依赖该特征”的解读不可靠。作者希望建立一个在语义损伤上可比的评估标准，以更准确衡量模型对形状、纹理与颜色等特征的依赖。

Method: 提出“语义匹配”的特征抑制评估：对形状抑制与纹理抑制分别调节强度，使二者在类别可分性(semantic separability)的损失上匹配，然后比较模型的性能下降。实验在ImageNet上，对CNN与ViT等架构进行对比；并进行脑编码分析，测量在抑制条件下预测人类视觉皮层神经反应的变化。

Result: 在语义匹配条件下，ImageNet训练的CNN对纹理抑制更敏感，性能下降大于形状抑制；跨架构比较显示，ViT在两类抑制下保持更高准确率；脑编码结果表明，在相同抑制设定下，ViT表征的神经预测性能下降更小。

Conclusion: 解释特征依赖时必须确保抑制操作在语义层面的可比性；在该框架下，CNN更依赖纹理，而ViT展现出更强的鲁棒性与更接近人类视觉皮层的表征特性，可能解释其稳健性优势。

Abstract: Understanding whether visual recognition models rely on shape, texture, or color is central to interpreting their behavior. Prior cue-conflict studies have strongly influenced the view that CNNs are texture-biased, yet such tests measure cue preference under artificial conflicts rather than feature reliance during natural recognition. We revisit this question through controlled feature suppression and show that performance drops are difficult to interpret unless different suppression operations impose comparable category-level damage. We introduce a semantically matched evaluation framework that compares shape and texture suppression at matched levels of category separability loss. Under this framework, ImageNet-trained CNNs show stronger degradation under texture suppression than under shape suppression, revealing greater texture reliance than suggested by unmatched suppression analyses. Extending the comparison across architectures, we find that Vision Transformers retain higher accuracy than CNNs under both shape and texture suppression. Brain encoding further shows that ViT representations exhibit smaller suppression-induced decreases in neural prediction performance under the tested suppression settings. These findings indicate that semantic comparability is essential for interpreting feature reliance from suppression experiments, and suggest that the robustness advantage of ViTs may be related to representations more compatible with human visual cortex.

### [20] [FedDP-PALD: A Privacy-Preserving Federated Latent Diffusion Framework with Prototype Aggregation for Medical Data Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16300)
*Md. Sajeebul Islam Sk.,Khan Enaet Hossain,Md. Mehedi Hasan Shawon*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FedDP-PALD：一种在差分隐私保障下进行多模态（胸片+ECG）数据合成与联邦学习的潜变量扩散框架，并配套DP-PMA聚合，既保性能又抗成员推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习可避免原始数据共享，但训练过程中的信息交换仍可能泄露成员身份；以合成数据替代真实数据常丢失预测结构，影响临床可用性。需要既能保护隐私又能保留判别信息的多模态生成-训练方案。

Conclusion: FedDP-PALD能在严格DP下生成保留判别性的多模态私有潜在表示，显著抵抗成员推断，同时保持较高临床预测性能，适用于跨院多模态医疗场景与缺失模态情况。

Abstract: Medical images and physiological signals provide valuable information for accurate diagnosis. Developing diagnostic models often requires patient data from multiple institutions, although strict privacy regulations limit the sharing of sensitive clinical records. Federated learning enables multiple hospitals to train a shared model without exchanging raw data. However, existing methods face two problems: the information exchanged during training can reveal whether a patient's data were used, and synthetic data meant to replace real records often fail to preserve their predictive structure, which limits clinical use. To address this issue, we propose FedDP-PALD, a privacy-preserving federated latent diffusion framework for multimodal medical data synthesis under formal privacy guarantees. It jointly processes chest X-ray images and electrocardiogram (ECG) signals through gated multi-head attention with modality-availability masks, remaining effective even when a modality is missing. We also introduce Differentially Private Prototype Mixture Aggregation (DP-PMA), which clips class-level latent prototypes and adds calibrated Gaussian noise before combining them on the server to maintain $(ε, δ)$ differential privacy. We evaluate FedDP-PALD on PneumoniaMNIST, ChestMNIST, and MIT-BIH datasets, where differential privacy reduced summary-level attack AUROC from 0.6229 $\pm$ 0.0026 to between 0.5016 and 0.5093 for privacy budgets from $ε= 1$ to $ε= 8$. On the test data, synthetic-latent training achieved an F1 score of 0.8993 $\pm$ 0.0006 and an AUROC of 0.9057 $\pm$ 0.0503, close to the 0.9747 $\pm$ 0.0132 real-latent training. These results show that FedDP-PALD generates private synthetic representations that preserve useful decision performance while strongly resisting membership inference.

### [21] [Med-OPD: Improving Medical Vision-Language Models via Evidence-Aware On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16303)
*Yunhang Qian,Jiaquan Yu,Jiawei Liu,Meng Wang,Hongwei Bran Li,Xiaobin Hu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Med-OPD：在医疗视觉语言模型中，用证据感知的在策略蒸馏强化对关键视觉证据的依赖，优于SFT与标准OPD。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Med-VLM常凭语言先验或模板产生“看似合理”的答案，而未真正关注诊断关键的细粒度视觉证据。标准在策略蒸馏(OPD)虽能隐私友好地迁移能力，但对所有token一视同仁，导致依赖证据的稀疏token被海量叙事token稀释。需要一种能在蒸馏过程中聚焦医学证据、提升多模态推理可靠性的框架。

Method: 提出Med-OPD：将OPD与医学证据感知监督统一后训练。核心为Medical Evidence Advantage(MEA)：给教师模型提供“答案感知”的提示，聚焦支持目标诊断的证据，并比较教师在原始与“证据退化”影像下的token似然，量化每个token对视觉证据的依赖。基于MEA，在token层与轨迹层重分配蒸馏权重，强化诊断关键token与依赖证据的rollout。

Result: 在OmniMedVQA各子集(CT、MRI、疾病诊断、病灶分级)上，Med-OPD稳定超越SFT与标准OPD，显示其能更好强化模型对关键视觉证据的依赖与多模态医学推理表现。

Conclusion: 证据感知的在策略蒸馏能缓解语言先验主导问题，使Med-VLM更可靠地基于关键视觉证据推理；Med-OPD提供了统一、隐私兼容的后训练路径，并在多数据集上验证有效性。

Abstract: Medical Vision-Language Models (Med-VLMs) require reliable reasoning from fine-grained visual evidence, yet existing models can produce plausible clinical answers by relying on language priors or medical templates rather than truly attending to diagnosis-critical regions. On-Policy Distillation (OPD) offers dense token-level supervision on student-generated trajectories and provides a privacy-compatible means of capability transfer without requiring the redistribution of raw patient data. However, standard OPD uniformly distills all tokens, causing sparse evidence-dependent tokens to be diluted by abundant clinical narrative tokens. Inspired by the success of OPD in the large language model community, we propose \textbf{Med-OPD}, to our knowledge the first unified post-training framework that integrates on-policy distillation with medical evidence-aware supervision for Med-VLMs. We introduce \textbf{Medical Evidence Advantage} (MEA), a teacher-grounded counterfactual signal that uses an answer-aware hint to focus teacher scoring on evidence supporting the target diagnosis, and measures each token's dependence on medical visual evidence by comparing teacher likelihoods under the original and evidence-degraded imaging modalities. Based on MEA, Med-OPD redistributes the distillation signal at both the token and trajectory levels, emphasizing diagnosis-critical tokens and evidence-reliant rollouts. Experiments on OmniMedVQA subsets show that Med-OPD consistently outperforms SFT and standard OPD across CT, MRI, Disease Diagnosis, and Lesion Grading. These results demonstrate that evidence-aware distillation can better strengthen medical VLMs' reliance on key visual evidence and improve reliable multimodal medical reasoning. The source code and data is publicly available at: https://github.com/yunhang8658/MedOPD.git

### [22] [Dual-Domain Self-Supervised Artifact Removal Framework for Photoacoustic Computed Tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16304)

TL;DR: 提出一种自监督的伪影去除框架，利用轻量级孪生网络与跨域一致性损失，在稀疏采样PACT重建中显著抑制伪影并保持高效计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PACT在稀疏探测条件下易出现严重重建伪影；传统反投影与傅里叶域方法产生的伪影模式差异显著，蕴含可互补的先验与约束，激发跨域协同学习以消除伪影、提升鲁棒性与效率的需求。

Method: 构建轻量级孪生神经网络，输入分别为基于反投影与傅里叶重建的两幅图。设计复合损失：跨域保真项以保持各自物理域的真实信息；不确定性加权一致性项以根据预测不确定度自适应对齐两域特征，从而解耦双域特征并滤除伪影。通过加速的空域/频域逆算子实现端到端快速推理。

Result: 在仿真、体模、活体大鼠及人体数据上验证，可显著抑制伪影、提升图像质量；受益于加速的逆算子与轻量模型，整体推理具有卓越的计算效率。

Conclusion: 跨域自监督孪生框架能有效利用反投影与傅里叶重建的互补性，在无GT标注下大幅降低PACT稀疏采样伪影，并以端到端方式实现高效高质重建。

Abstract: Photoacoustic Computed Tomography (PACT) often faces severe challenges from reconstruction artifacts due to sparse detection conditions. In this work, based on the distinct differences in artifact patterns between back-projection-based and Fourier-based reconstruction algorithms, we propose a self-supervised artifact removal framework that employs a lightweight Siamese Neural Network and a composite loss function integrating cross-domain fidelity and uncertainty-weighted consistency, effectively decoupling dual-domain features and filtering artifacts. Comprehensive validations using simulations, phantoms, in vivo rat and human experimental data demonstrate that the proposed method can significantly suppress image artifacts. Furthermore, enabled by the acceleration of the spatial-domain and frequency-domain inverse operator, this end-to-end approach also achieves exceptional computational efficiency.

### [23] [LookME: Lookup-Based Multimodal Embeddings for Layer Injection in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16305)
*Zeyu Xu,Xingzhong Hou,Pengkai Guo,Siling Lin,Xiao Xu,Menghua Zhai,Haoyu Chen,Yunke Zhang,Fei Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出LookME：在VLM中对多模态连续嵌入进行查表增强的首个框架，利用分层（场景→原语）两级查找与稀疏注入＋跨层表复用，实现按需加载、参数可扩展与高效推理，在多项视觉基准上优于仅文本的PLE方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM若靠密集或稀疏MoE扩展，面临内存与时延权衡：全加载显存高、按需加载延迟大。PLE通过大外部嵌入表ROM查找增强，但主要面向文本ID检索，不适合包含更丰富连续特征的多模态（视觉）嵌入，限制了在VLM中的效果与可扩展性。

Method: 提出LookME框架，使VLM支持对大规模多模态嵌入表进行查表增强并可分区存储、按需加载。核心是分层两级查找：先粗粒度场景级检索，再细粒度场景内原语级精检，从连续嵌入中高效定位相关条目；并配合稀疏注入策略，仅在需要处注入关键嵌入，且在相邻层间复用嵌入表，提升效率、模型规模与性能的折中。

Result: 在多项视觉数据集上，LookME优于仅文本PLE风格方法，证明多模态查表增强的有效性；同时在效率（按需加载、较低延迟）与模型大小（外部表ROM化、跨层复用）方面达到更优权衡。

Conclusion: LookME实现了面向VLM的多模态连续嵌入查表增强，通过分层检索与稀疏注入兼顾性能与资源效率，克服了文本型PLE在多模态场景的局限。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved strong progress in multimodal understanding. However, scaling dense or sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models to improve performance limits deployment in resource-constrained environments due to the trade-off between high memory usage from full loading and increased latency from on-demand loading. Recently, the Per-Layer Embedding (PLE) architecture addresses this by scaling models with large external embedding tables stored in ROM and performing lightweight lookup to retrieve relevant embeddings to enhance token representations. Nevertheless, existing PLE-style methods are primarily designed for text embeddings due to the convenience of ID-based retrieval, limiting their effectiveness in VLMs where multimodal embeddings contain richer information for visual tasks. In this paper, we propose LookME, the first framework that enables lookup-based enhancement for multimodal embeddings in VLMs while supporting partitioned storage and on-demand loading. To efficiently lookup arbitrary continuous multimodal embeddings from large-scale embedding tables, we propose a hierarchical two-level lookup method employing a coarse-to-fine strategy that performs lookups from the scene-level to the intra-scene primitive-level. Furthermore, we integrate the lookup method with a sparse injection strategy, which adaptively prioritizes critical embeddings over voluminous multimodal embeddings within layers, and facilitates embedding table reuse across neighboring layers, improving the trade-off among efficiency, model size, and performance. Experiments on multiple visual benchmarks show that LookME outperforms text-only PLE-style methods, validating the effectiveness of lookup-based multimodal embedding enhancement.

### [24] [CoBind: Stage-Aware Compositional Binding for Training-Free Text-to-Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16307)
*Kaijie Chen,Ethan Caldwell,Mira Vossen,Julian Hartwell,Serena Whitlock,Adrian Bellamy*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CoBind是一种训练免的分阶段组合约束绑定框架，通过将文本解析为实体-属性-关系图，在早期稳固全局布局与关系，中期对属性进行跨实体对比绑定，后期逐步放松结构引导，从而显著提升多实体、多属性与空间关系生成的一致性，同时保持画面细节与质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散文生图在复杂提示（多实体、多属性、关系）上常出现漏物体、属性错配、空间关系颠倒等问题；训练免方法多仅增强token注意力，缺乏显式“哪个属性属于哪个实体、在去噪哪一阶段约束什么”的机制。

Method: 1) 将提示解析为由实体、属性、关系构成的组合图；2) 早期去噪阶段：通过实体完备性与关系约束先确立全局布局；3) 中期：采用跨实体对比式优化，将属性与其目标实体进行绑定，抑制错配；4) 后期：逐步放松结构引导以保留纹理与细节；5) 动态调节各约束强度，依据当前满足度自适应减少不必要的潜空间更新；全程无需再训练或额外标注，兼容多种扩散骨干。

Result: 在T2I-CompBench++、GenEval及多种扩散模型上，属性绑定、空间关系与复杂组合生成的一致性均有稳定提升，且视觉质量保持竞争力。

Conclusion: 通过分阶段、结构感知与自适应强度的训练免绑定，CoBind有效弥补了现有方法对复杂组合提示的不足，提升可控性与一致性而不牺牲细节与通用性。

Abstract: Diffusion-based text-to-image models often fail on complex prompts involving multiple entities, attributes, and relations, producing object omissions, incorrect attribute assignments, or reversed spatial layouts. Existing training-free methods mainly strengthen token-level attention, but do not explicitly model which attributes belong to which entities or when different constraints should be enforced during denoising.
  We introduce \textbf{CoBind}, a training-free framework for stage-aware compositional binding. CoBind parses a prompt into a composition graph of entities, attributes, and relations. It first establishes the global layout using entity-completeness and relation constraints, then binds attributes to their target entities through contrastive cross-entity optimization. Structural guidance is gradually relaxed in later denoising steps to preserve textures and visual details. CoBind also adapts the guidance strength according to the current satisfaction of each constraint, reducing unnecessary latent updates.
  CoBind requires no retraining or additional annotations. Experiments on T2I-CompBench++, GenEval, and multiple diffusion backbones show consistent improvements in attribute binding, spatial relations, and complex compositional generation while maintaining competitive visual quality.

</details>


### [25] [DAUPNet: Domain-Aware Uncertainty Modeling for Reliable Prototype Discrimination in Cross-Domain Few-Shot Semantic Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16308)
*Lei Yuan,Zhongxu Hu,Jingyi Wen,Pengxing Yi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DAUPNet，将跨域原型匹配重构为“面向不确定性的原型判别”，在四个目标域上显著提升CD-FSS性能（1/5-shot平均mIoU达72.6%/76.7%），尤其在医疗域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CD-FSS多依赖域不变表示或改进支撑-查询对应，但大域移导致原型匹配不可靠：层级响应不一致污染支撑表示；确定性原型难以表达边界与外观歧义；不同置信度的原型在优化中被等价对待，削弱前景/背景分离。

Method: 提出DAUPNet的三步统一框架：1) 层级特征协调：对齐并和谐化支撑-查询的多层级特征，提供稳定证据；2) 概率原型：以前景/背景的概率分布建模原型，显式表征不确定性（边界、外观变化）；3) 不确定性感知对比优化：利用估计的不确定性加权或调节对比学习目标，使可靠原型贡献更大、噪声原型影响减弱。

Result: 在四个标准目标域上，1-shot与5-shot平均mIoU分别达到72.6%与76.7%，在两个医疗域获得显著增益，表明方法在严重域移下稳健有效。

Conclusion: 通过建模并利用原型不确定性，结合层级特征协调与不确定性感知优化，可实现更鲁棒、可解释的跨域小样本语义分割。代码已开源：github.com/madness-Lei/DAUPNet。

Abstract: Cross-domain few-shot semantic segmentation (CD-FSS) has predominantly been formulated as learning domain-invariant representations or improving support-query correspondence. Nevertheless, large domain shifts still make prototype matching unreliable: inconsistent hierarchical responses corrupt the support representation, deterministic prototypes cannot express boundary and appearance ambiguity, and treating prototypes with different reliability equally during optimization weakens foreground-background separation. We therefore propose DAUPNet, a unified framework that reformulates cross-domain prototype matching as uncertainty-aware prototype discrimination. DAUPNet first harmonizes hierarchical support-query features to provide stable evidence, then represents foreground and background prototypes probabilistically, and finally uses their estimated uncertainty to regulate contrastive optimization. On four standard target domains, DAUPNet achieves 72.6% and 76.7% average mIoU in the 1-shot and 5-shot settings, respectively, including substantial gains on the two medical domains. These results demonstrate that modeling prototype uncertainty and incorporating it into optimization provides a robust and interpretable approach to CD-FSS under severe domain shift. The code is available at https://github.com/madness-Lei/DAUPNet

</details>


### [26] [SaaF: Scene-Specific Ambiguity-Aware 3D Language Fields towards Interactive Real-World Object Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16309)
*Yuga Yano,Daiju Kanaoka,Hakaru Tamukoh,Yasutomo Kawanishi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SaaF 提出一种基于高斯泼洒的场景专属3D语言场，用于真实场景中的交互式自然语言目标检索；通过度量学习构建同时“区分实例”和“感知歧义”的统一特征空间，从而在开放词汇下提升检索准确性并能检测并处理模糊查询。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D语言场将渲染像素与经自编码器压缩的CLIP特征对齐，导致：1) 压缩引起相似物体可分性下降；2) 对含糊文本处理差，易产生不稳定或错误检索。服务机器人在复杂真实环境中需要既能细粒度识别又能与用户就歧义交互澄清的能力。

Method: 提出Scene-specific Ambiguity-aware 3D Language Fields (SaaF)。核心是度量学习统一特征空间：i) 实例判别：将同一物体多视角图像特征在特征空间中拉近，增强实例级区分；ii) 歧义建模：对每个被跟踪的物体图像序列，生成多种文本标签（包含模糊与具体描述），联合训练以学习场景内模糊与具体语义间的关系。采用高斯泼洒表示的3D语言场以支持渲染—文本对齐与交互式检索，并可估计查询歧义、触发澄清。

Result: 在开放词汇设置下，相比以往方法，SaaF在检索准确率上有提升，并能稳定检测并处理用户文本查询中的歧义。

Conclusion: 通过度量学习和多粒度文本联合训练，SaaF在场景专属3D语言场中实现了更强的实例判别与歧义感知能力，支持交互式澄清并提升真实场景目标检索的可靠性与准确性。

Abstract: We propose Scene-specific Ambiguity-aware 3D Language Fields (SaaF), a novel Gaussian Splatting-based 3D language field designed for interactive object retrieval in a given real-world scene. Interactive object retrieval using natural language is a crucial capability for service robots operating in complex real-world environments. While recent 3D language field methods for object retrieval establish associations between rendered pixels and autoencoder-compressed CLIP features, they suffer from two limitations: (1) reduced discriminability among similar objects due to feature compression, and (2) poor handling of ambiguous queries, often resulting in unstable or incorrect retrieval. To address these limitations, SaaF introduces a metric learning strategy to construct a unified feature space that is both instance-discriminative and ambiguity-aware. (i) To enhance instance-level visual discrimination, SaaF employs metric learning that pulls image features from multiple viewpoints of the same object closer together in the feature space. (ii) To establish ambiguity awareness, the model jointly trains on multiple text labels generated by the proposed method from each tracked object image sequence, including ambiguous descriptions, to learn the semantic relationships between ambiguous and specific features in a target scene. This feature space enables fine-grained visual understanding while allowing the system to estimate query ambiguity and interactively request clarification when needed. Experimental results demonstrate that SaaF not only improves retrieval accuracy over previous methods but also robustly detects and handles ambiguity in the user text queries under open-vocabulary settings.

### [27] [Seeing What Is Actually There: PriVE-Bench and PriVE-Tools for Counterfactual Evaluation of Agentic Visual Evidence in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16311)
*Jingyu Sun,Jiachen Tu,Yuyang Xue,Yaoxin Jiang,Guoyi Xu,Zhengtao Yao,Rui Qian,Yizheng Sun,Hongpeng Zhou,Jingyuan Sun,Yan Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PriVE-Bench与PriVE-Tools，评估并增强VLM在反事实场景下对视觉证据的落地性；工具证据有助于但非万能，许多模型仍受语言/类别先验支配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM常依赖语言与类别先验而非像素证据，尤其在反事实图像中会给出“看似常识”的错误答案。现有基准多仅检测是否存在先验依赖，缺乏对在多视图与工具辅助下能否克服先验的系统评估。

Method: 构建PriVE-Bench：成对（原始/反事实）图像，区分基于视觉落地的回答与遵循先验的错误；提出PriVE-Tools：提供可控的、类代理式视觉工具证据（框选、裁剪、放大面板、轮廓），评测在相同反事实冲突下，这些证据是否提升落地性。对开源与闭源VLM在三种输入设定（原始、成对图像、工具条件）下，报告准确率、先验跟随错误率、其他回答率。

Result: 工具化视觉证据在部分情境下提升表现，尤其当模型能有效利用局部化证据时；但改进并不普适，即便显式提供相关证据，多数模型仍会受语言/类别先验驱动而出错。

Conclusion: 提供了评估与分析VLM先验依赖与视觉落地性的框架。工具证据可缓解但难以根治先验偏置；未来需在模型训练与推理机制上改进，使其在反事实冲突中更可靠地依赖像素证据。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) often answer visual questions using learned language and category priors rather than grounding their predictions in the image itself. Counterfactual images provide a natural diagnostic setting for this failure mode: when visible evidence contradicts what is usually true, a grounded model should answer from the pixels, while a prior-following model will produce a canonical but visually incorrect response. However, existing counterfactual benchmarks mainly ask whether such prior-following behavior exists. In this paper, we ask a further question motivated by the rise of tool-augmented and agentic vision systems: can additional visual evidence views help VLMs reason against their priors? We introduce PriVE-Bench, a Prior-vs-Visual Evidence Benchmark that uses paired original and counterfactual images to distinguish visually grounded answers from prior-consistent errors. We further introduce PriVE-Tools, a controlled agentic-vision-inspired extension that evaluates whether tool-derived visual evidence -- including bounding boxes, crops, zoom panels, and contours -- improves grounding under the same counterfactual conflicts. Across open- and closed-source VLMs, we compare raw, paired-image, and tool-conditioned inputs using accuracy, prior-following error rate, and other-response rate. Our results show that visual evidence tools can help in some settings, especially when models can use localized evidence effectively, but they are not a universal remedy: several models continue to follow language and category priors even when relevant visual evidence is explicitly provided.

Abstract: The transition toward high-mix low-volume manufacturing demands flexibility in robotic manipulation. Validated at a TRL of 6, the core methodology behind xperception is based on the FreeZe algorithm, which won the international BOP Challenge 2024, paving the way for scalable, plug-and-play robotic automation in unstructured high-mix low-volume manufacturing industries.

### [29] [Depth-Regularized JEPA World Models Learn More Transferable Representations from Real Outdoor Robot Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16314)
*Usman M. Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出在JEPA世界模型训练中引入“深度”几何先验与各向同性潜变量正则（SIGReg），并配合仅训练期的过参数化，使模型在复杂真实户外视频上学到更鲁棒的潜在动力学而不增加推理开销。对农机机器人视频训练的18M参数模型，在冻结表征的视觉里程计、基于预测器的意外值检测、以及多步潜在rollout保真度上，较LeWM显著提升：里程计误差-33%，意外分数分离在域内与TartanGround OOD均增强，长跨度rollout在域移下更稳健；并且对非纯几何因素（光照/阴影）的意外分离也改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有JEPA世界模型虽能学到稳健动力学，但在视觉复杂、不可预测的真实户外场景（如农业机器人）上仍易受干扰。需要引入物理上有依据的先验，帮助模型在保持紧凑与推理高效的同时，提升表征的通用性与可迁移性。

Method: 在JEPA框架中加入：1) 深度监督作为几何先验，引导潜在表征与场景几何一致；2) 各向同性诱导的潜在正则SIGReg，在最大化与任务无关的潜在多样性的同时，约束其组织方式以获得最高熵且受几何约束的表征；3) 仅训练期过参数化以容纳更高复杂度但不增加推理时复杂度。使用真实农业机器人视频训练一个18M参数模型；评估通过冻结表征的视觉里程计探针、基于预测器的“惊讶度”检测、及多步潜在rollout保真度。

Result: 相较LeWM基线：视觉里程计探针误差降低33%；在域内与TartanGround OOD基准上，惊讶度分数分离显著增大；多步潜在rollout在域移下保真度提升，且随rollout步长增加而优势扩大；并在与3D几何不直接相关的物理因素（如光照、阴影）上的惊讶度分离同样得到改进。

Conclusion: 以深度为物理几何先验、配合SIGReg与训练期过参数化，可以在不增加推理开销的前提下，使紧凑的JEPA世界模型在真实户外数据上学到更可迁移、更通用的强表征，提升多种下游与评测任务的表现；深度先验有望推广以增强世界模型在多任务中的泛化。

Abstract: World models, especially based on JEPA architectures, have been shown to learn robust dynamics of various environments. However, learning from visually complex real-world data remains a challenge, especially in unpredictable outdoor environments. We introduce depth as a geometric prior during training in learning more robust latent dynamics directly from robot video data and handling visual complexity. This combines depth supervision with an isotropy-inducing latent regularizer (SIGReg), maximizing task-agnostic latent diversity while constraining how that diversity is organized, with the combined objective targeting the highest-entropy representation consistent with scene geometry. To satisfy this greater complexity without increasing inference time, we also add training-only overparameterization. Training an 18M-parameter model on video from a real agricultural robot, we evaluate with frozen-representation visual odometry probes, predictor-based surprise detection, and multi-step latent rollout fidelity. Compared to the baseline LeWM, our method lowers visual odometry probe error by 33%, substantially increases surprise-score separation both in-domain and on the out-of-domain TartanGround benchmark, and improves multi-step rollout fidelity under domain shift, with gains that grow with rollout horizon. Notably, we also see improvements in surprise-score separation on physics understanding that is not directly tied to 3D geometry, such as lighting and shadows. These results show that a lightweight training-time geometric prior makes a compact JEPA world model more useful and more transferable on real outdoor data with strong underlying representations, without adding inference overhead. Our work suggests that depth as a physically grounded prior can enhance world model generalization on a variety of tasks.

</details>


### [30] [Eddy-VL 1.9B: Structural Pruning and Layered Distillation for Edge-Deployable Multimodal Embedding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16316)
*HanYeong Cho,Changwoo Kim,Taeuk Chu,Jimin Park*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Eddy-VL 1.9B 是在 Qwen3-VL-Embedding-2B 基础上通过结构剪枝与分层蒸馏压缩得到的离线多模态嵌入模型，面向无网低时延取证与检索；在保留约91.7%性能的同时，参数降约9.5%，推理时延降约10%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在取证/调查等空隔离与边缘部署场景中，无法依赖云端大模型推理，但仍需高质量图文检索与推理能力，且对延迟与内存占用敏感。因此需要在不显著牺牲效果的前提下压缩多模态嵌入模型，实现本地、低时延、可部署。

Method: 两阶段压缩：1) 探针驱动的结构化深度剪枝：用相邻层线性CKA排名，从文本解码器中移除4层（28→24）。2) 分层知识蒸馏：采用“补洞式”师生层映射，中层用注意力图1-CKA对齐，末层结合MSE与余弦损失，并采用套娃（Matryoshka）多维度嵌入{128,256,512,1024,2048}训练。

Result: 模型参数降至1.926B（约3.85GB bf16，较教师2.13B降约9.5%）。在MMEB-V2（78任务，VLM2Vec协议）总体得分63.2，对比教师68.9，保留91.7%性能；相较仅剪枝后的56.8，通过蒸馏追回6.4/12.1分。组合推理保持接近：SugarCrepe 86.1 vs 86.4、MR2-Bench 24.5 vs 24.7、ARO 59.5 vs 60.4；Winoground组仍偏弱：6.8 vs 8.5。深度剪枝使单图前向时延降约10%（150.0→136.4ms，DGX Spark + FlashAttention-2）。

Conclusion: Eddy-VL 1.9B 以小幅参数与时延代价实现高保真度的多模态检索能力，适配离线边缘部署；结构剪枝+分层蒸馏的组合在维持组合推理方面有效，但对Winoground仍是瓶颈。权重与推理代码已开放，适合在受限环境下进行多模态检索应用。

Abstract: In this report, we introduce Eddy-VL 1.9B, a compressed multimodal embedding model built on Qwen3-VL-Embedding-2B for offline, edge-deployable vision-language retrieval. Eddy-VL targets air-gapped forensic and investigative settings where cloud APIs are unavailable and low latency is essential. Compression combines (i) probe-driven structural pruning that removes four redundant text-decoder layers (28 to 24) ranked by adjacent-layer linear CKA, and (ii) layered knowledge distillation with hole-covering teacher-student mappings, mid-layer attention-map 1-CKA, and final-layer MSE and cosine losses with Matryoshka dimensions {128, 256, 512, 1024, 2048}. The released model contains 1,926,188,032 parameters (3.85 GB bf16), representing approximately 9.5% fewer parameters than the 2.13B teacher model. Empirical evaluations on MMEB-V2 (78 tasks, VLM2Vec protocol) show that Eddy-VL achieves an overall score of 63.2 compared with 68.9 for the teacher, retaining 91.7% of the teacher's performance while recovering 6.4 of the 12.1 points lost through pruning alone (56.8). Compositional reasoning performance remains close to the teacher on SugarCrepe (86.1 vs. 86.4), MR2-Bench (24.5 vs. 24.7), and ARO (59.5 vs. 60.4), while Winoground group performance (6.8 vs. 8.5) remains the primary limitation. Depth pruning also reduces forward latency by approximately 10% (150.0 to 136.4 ms per image on NVIDIA DGX Spark using FlashAttention-2). We present the architecture, compression methodology, training procedures, and evaluation results, demonstrating the effectiveness of Eddy-VL for multimodal retrieval under constrained edge deployment. Model weights and inference code are publicly available on Hugging Face.

### [31] [Monte Carlo Dropout Uncertainty and Entropy-Thresholded Selective Prediction for Architecture-Agnostic Brain Tumor MRI Triage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16317)
*Medhansh Sharma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出基于MC Dropout的不确定性优先管线，用温度缩放校准，并据熵制定“转人工”规则；在去重划分的MRI四分类任务上，强判别、良好校准，少量延迟可显著提升有效准确率，且与架构无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床落地的关键不是最高准确率，而是能否可靠识别模型不自信、易错的病例并转交放射科医师。常规确定性置信度（如并训的置信头）会塌缩为近常数，无法指示正确性，需要能度量并利用预测不确定性的方案。

Method: 在脑肿瘤MRI四分类（神经胶质瘤、脑膜瘤、垂体瘤、无肿瘤）中：1) 采用MC Dropout进行T=20次前向，基于预测分布熵量化不确定性；2) 用显式熵阈值作为转人工规则；3) 用感知哈希聚类分割7200张图像，避免近重复泄漏；4) 在ViT-B/16与ResNet-50上、5个随机种子下，从判别、校准、选择性预测三方面评估；5) 用单一温度缩放对确定性softmax做后验校准。

Result: 两种架构均表现强判别（宏AUC 0.994；准确率约0.962-0.964），不同种子间无显著差异（5/5不显著，p<0.05），表明性能主要来自不确定性管线而非网络本身；温度缩放后ECE约0.016-0.020；按熵延迟最不确定的5%病例，其余覆盖上的准确率约0.98；风险-覆盖曲线下面积约0.010-0.011。

Conclusion: MC Dropout产生的预测不确定性在该任务上已校准且不塌缩，可用明确的“延迟-转人工”规则直接行动；该流程与模型架构无关，为内部分验证条件下的经校准、可转人工的脑肿瘤MRI分诊提供可行基线。

Abstract: Deep networks now subtype brain tumors on MRI about as well as specialist readers, yet accuracy is not what keeps them out of the clinic. What matters at the point of care is whether a model's confidence can be trusted to flag the cases it is likely to misclassify and defer them to a human. Deterministic estimates cannot: an auxiliary confidence head trained alongside the classifier collapses to a near-constant output that says nothing about correctness. This study proposes an uncertainty-first pipeline for four-class brain tumor MRI (glioma, meningioma, pituitary, no tumor) that reads predictive uncertainty from Monte Carlo (MC) Dropout over T = 20 passes and turns the resulting entropy into an explicit rule for deferring uncertain cases to a radiologist. We partitioned 7,200 images by perceptual-hash cluster, closing the near-duplicate leakage that inflates accuracy under naive splitting, and evaluated the pipeline on ViT-B/16 and ResNet-50 across five seeds along three axes: discrimination, calibration, and selective prediction. Both discriminate strongly (macro-AUC 0.994; accuracy 0.962 and 0.964), and no seed separates them (0 of 5 significant, p < 0.05), so the result is driven by the uncertainty pipeline, not the network. A single temperature scalar pulls the deterministic softmax into tight calibration (expected calibration error 0.016-0.020), and deferring the most uncertain 5% of cases lifts accuracy on the rest to about 0.98 on both (area under the risk-coverage curve 0.010-0.011). MC-Dropout uncertainty here is thus calibrated, non-collapsing, and directly actionable through a concrete deferral rule, providing an architecture-agnostic basis for calibrated, defer-to-human brain tumor MRI triage under internal validation.

Abstract: As Ultra-High-Definition (UHD) displays and immersive media services become ubiquitous in the Internet of Things (IoT) and Consumer Electronics (CE) sectors, including 8K display and mobile devices, the demand for high-efficiency video coding is unprecedented. While Deep Learning-based Filtering (DLF) has emerged as a promising solution to mitigate compression artifacts inherent in standards like High Efficiency Video Coding (HEVC/H.265) and Versatile Video Coding (VVC/H.266), its deployment in CE devices is severely constrained by computational complexity, memory bandwidth, and power consumption. To bridge the gap between academic research and practical deployment, this paper presents a comprehensive, hardware-oriented survey of DLF techniques. We propose a systematic three-dimensional taxonomy classifying methods into (1) Integration Scheme within the Video Coding, (2) Coding Information Utilization, and (3) Network Design Strategy. Unlike prior reviews, this work critically analyzes the trade-offs between Rate-Distortion (RD) performance and hardware feasibility, highlighting the evolution from heavy, performance-oriented models to lightweight, hardware-friendly architectures targeting Neural Processing Units (NPUs). Furthermore, we incorporate the latest standardization activities from the Joint Video Experts Team (JVET) on Neural Network-based Video Coding (NNVC) to provide realistic guidelines. We also identify open challenges such as real-time inference latency and error propagation, providing a roadmap toward robust, low-power intelligent video coding in next-generation CE vision endpoints.

### [33] [The Devil is in the Dark Pixels: Toward Brightness Bias-Robust Denoising](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16320)
*Sungjun Cho,Zhuangzhuang Chen,Xiaomeng Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出在信号相关相机噪声下，暗区先天地位SNR低，MSE训练的去噪器因“亮度偏置”而对暗区恢复更差；提出BBRD损失：按亮度分组、按噪声方差归一化误差并用Group-DRO动态上调最差组权重，无额外推理开销；在多架构多数据上各亮度段均提升，暗区与总体PSNR显著提高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实相机噪声随信号强度变化，暗部信号衰减比噪声方差下降更快，导致SNR极低；现有以MSE为目标的网络在此设置下训练梯度被亮部主导，暗部被忽视，实测暗像素重建误差相对噪声下限可达6倍，迫切需要一种同时关注各亮度段、尤其暗区的训练目标。

Method: 提出BBRD（Brightness Bias-Robust Denoising）作为MSE的替代：1）将像素按亮度分桶（band）；2）对每个band的重建误差按该band的经验噪声方差进行归一化；3）采用Group Distributionally Robust Optimization，对当前最差表现的band自适应上权重，从而平衡梯度，抑制亮度引起的偏置。该方法无需新增参数与推理开销，可直接替换训练损失。作者还分析了偏置来源：信号相关噪声使亮部残差放大，且网络Jacobian范数随亮度单调增大，二者导致亮部主导更新。

Result: 在8个架构、2个数据集上与13种替代方法比较，BBRD是唯一能在所有亮度band上同时提升的方法：在SIDD上暗band最高+0.45 dB、亮band+0.32 dB、总体PSNR最高+0.65 dB；最大收益集中在最暗区域。

Conclusion: MSE训练在信号相关噪声下存在系统性的亮度偏置，使暗区去噪受损。BBRD通过按亮度分组、噪声归一化和Group-DRO动态重加权，有效纠偏并在不增加推理成本的前提下全面提升各亮度段的去噪质量，尤其改善暗部细节恢复。

Abstract: In this paper, we reveal an important yet overlooked problem in image denoising: under signal-dependent camera noise models, dark regions suffer from inherently low Signal-to-Noise Ratio (SNR), as signal intensity decays far faster than noise variance diminishes, making detail recovery in dark areas fundamentally challenging. Yet rather than compensating for this difficulty, MSE-trained denoisers exacerbate it -- reconstructing dark pixels up to 6x worse relative to their per-band noise floor. This bias stems from two compounding factors: signal-dependent noise inflates bright-pixel residuals, and the network's Jacobian norm increases monotonically with brightness. Together, these cause bright regions to chronically dominate gradient updates at the expense of dark ones. To this end, we propose Brightness Bias-Robust Denoising (BBRD), a drop-in replacement for MSE loss that partitions pixels into brightness bands, normalizes per-band error by empirical noise variance, and applies Group Distributionally Robust Optimization (Group-DRO) to dynamically upweight whichever band is currently worst, with zero additional parameters or inference cost. Across 8 architectures and 2 datasets in our experiments, BBRD is the only method among 13 tested alternatives that improves each brightness band simultaneously, achieving up to +0.45 dB on dark bands, +0.32 dB on bright bands, and +0.65 dB aggregate Peak Signal-to-Noise Ratio (PSNR) on SIDD, with the largest per-band gains in the darkest regions where detail recovery matters most. Code is available at https://github.com/xmed-lab/BBRD

</details>


### [34] [Art Beyond Semantics: Sheaf-Informed Contrastive Learning for Multi-Relational Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16321)
*Ludovica Schaerf,Antonio Purificato,Piera Riccio,Fabrizio Silvestri,Noa Garcia*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 受层析-层范（sheaf）思想启发，为每种关系上下文学习独立但可协调的嵌入通道：给定图像/文本和指定关系类型，将样本投影到对应的上下文嵌入；提出新的上下文对比损失，在训练时显式编码“同一对象在同一关系下应对齐、在不同关系下可区分”的约束；推理时无需外部知识。

Result: 在三个新构建的艺术多关系数据集（WikiArt+、HertzianaDP、SemArt+）上进行多模态检索与艺术理解评测，CANVAS均显著超过CLIP等基线。

Conclusion: 多关系对齐既有理论必要性也有实证价值；通过上下文条件化嵌入与对比学习，可更好捕捉艺术品在不同解读维度下的视觉-文本对应关系，提升检索与理解性能。

Abstract: Understanding a painting is never a single act. Art historians may analyze the same work through concepts of style, iconography, or historical context, dimensions that are not interchangeable, and each carries distinct semantic relationships between the visual and the textual. Vision-Language Models (VLMs) like CLIP, which learn a single shared embedding space, collapse this richness into a single homogeneous alignment, thereby losing the multi-relational structure that defines art-historical reasoning. We introduce CANVAS (Contrastive Art-aware Network for Vision-Language Alignment with Sheaves), a framework for learning relation-aware multimodal representations inspired by sheaf theory. Each artwork is projected into multiple embeddings conditioned on the type of relation (i.e., the context), and a novel contrastive loss encodes contextual information during training, with no dependency on external data at inference. We evaluate on three newly introduced benchmarks of artworks for multi-relational art understanding: WikiArt+, derived from WikiArt and Wikipedia, HertzianaDP, from the Bibliotheca Hertziana collection, and SemArt+, refined from the SemArt dataset. In multimodal retrieval and art understanding, CANVAS outperforms the baselines, supporting the view that multi-relational alignment is not just theoretically motivated but also practically essential.

Abstract: Micro-gesture recognition demands the detection of fleeting, spatially localized movements that are frequently overwhelmed by dominant static appearances and background noise. While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) excel at general video understanding, they inherently struggle with subtle kinematics and often rely on static posture priors. To this end, we propose GMoT, a Gated Motion-Aware Tokenization module that explicitly distills sparse kinematic evidence into a compact sequence prior to temporal modeling. GMoT dynamically spotlights action-relevant regions via spatially weighted pooling, extracts adjacent-frame temporal differencing to capture precise motion energy, and adaptively fuses these cues into the visual stream using a conservatively initialized semantic gate. To transition from simple classification to evidence-grounded reasoning, we further introduce a progressive reward-guided policy refinement paradigm, supported by a semi-supervised annotation pipeline that generates anatomically focused captions. ### [36] [SGMCE: Segment-Grounded Morphological Concept Explanation for Malaria Parasite Species Identification in Thick Blood Smears](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16324)
