### [84] [InfoDense: Density-Aware Regional Decisive Replay for Memory-Efficient Incremental Face Forgery Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16873)
*Jikang Cheng,Hao Shen,Xueyi Zhang,Guangcheng Wang,Zhongyuan Wang,Renye Yan,Baojin Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出InfoDense，一种密度感知、区域决策式重放策略，用于增量人脸伪造检测，在有限内存下优先保留伪迹密集与关键区域，通过剪取、选择与融合三步减少灾难性遗忘并提升跨域泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 增量人脸伪造检测需要在不断出现的新型伪造下更新模型，但传统基于重放的方法在内存受限时要么存不住细微伪迹、要么引入域偏差，导致遗忘与泛化差。需要一种在小存储下仍能保留“可迁移伪造证据”的数据选择与使用策略。

Method: 提出InfoDense三阶段：1) InfoDense Cut：利用CLIP嵌入定位并裁剪含伪造伪迹最密集、最具判别力的小块；2) InfoDense Select：在潜空间代表性与关键块计数的联合评分下，对候选片段排序与筛选，保证多样性与信息密度；3) InfoDense Fuse：将历史选中片段与当前任务样本自适应融合，构造无偏输入，协助知识保持与泛化。

Result: 在具有挑战性的增量深伪基准上，方法显著降低灾难性遗忘，并在跨域测试中优于传统重放方案，达到更高的检测性能与稳定性（文中称“广泛实验”验证）。

Conclusion: 面向IFFD，关注“伪迹密度与关键区域”的重放比存整图更高效；通过裁剪—选择—融合的流水线，可在小内存下保留高保真伪造证据，缓解遗忘并提升跨域泛化。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of face forgery techniques has introduced an increasing variety of manipulations. Incremental Face Forgery Detection (IFFD), which incrementally adds new forgery data to fine-tune previously trained models, has emerged as a promising approach to handle evolving forgery threats. However, conventional replay-based IFFD methods suffer from catastrophic forgetting. Storing full historical images under limited memory often either fails to preserve subtle forgery cues or introduces domain bias, reducing the model's ability to learn intrinsic and transferable manipulation characteristics. In this paper, we propose a Density-Aware Regional Decisive replay strategy, termed InfoDense, to address these challenges. InfoDense prioritizes artifact-dense and forgery-critical regions, significantly reducing storage requirements while maintaining high-fidelity forgery evidence. We first introduce InfoDense Cut to localize decisive patches using CLIP-based embeddings. Then, InfoDense Select ranks candidate segments by combining latent-space representativeness and decisive patch counts, ensuring both diversity and information density in the replay buffer. Finally, InfoDense Fuse reconstructs unbiased training inputs by adaptively merging stored segments with current-task samples, enhancing knowledge retention and generalization. Extensive experiments on challenging incremental deepfake benchmarks demonstrate that InfoDense effectively mitigates catastrophic forgetting while improving cross-domain generalization.

### [85] [Transferable Low-Rank Convolutional Bases for Onboarding Unseen Medical Imaging Modalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16888)
*Ranat Das Prangon,Istiaque Ahmed,Shajid Hasan Naim,Waseem Mustak Zisan,Hossain Md Shakhawat*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文研究在不重新训练主干网络的情况下，为医疗影像模型接入全新模态（如在CT/MRI上训练后接入X光）的“在岗扩容（onboarding）”问题，并提出使用卷积LoRA及其可迁移的低秩卷积基来实现高效适配，保持源模态性能不变，同时在目标模态上获得接近全量微调的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际部署中，已上线的多模态医学影像模型常需后续支持从未见过的新模态。全面微调代价高且会破坏已服务模态的性能（灾难性遗忘）。需要一种参数高效、不会损伤已学能力、还能对全新模态有效适配的技术路径。

Method: 采用严格的留一域（模态）外协议：用肾脏CT与脑部MRI预训练并冻结卷积主干，然后在胸部X光上仅做轻量适配。系统比较：线性探针、全连接层LoRA、卷积LoRA；提出并验证“低秩卷积基”在源模态上学习后可迁移：冻结该基，仅训练其上投影以适配新模态；评估源/目标精度权衡，并用冻结主干特征的马氏距离分数检测未见模态作为触发器。

Result: (1) 仅决策层微调不足：线性探针与FC-LoRA显著落后；卷积LoRA能恢复大部分可达精度，说明必须适配到卷积特征层。(2) 源模态上学得的低秩卷积“基”可迁移：冻结该基，仅训练上投影即可在目标模态上达到接近全量微调的性能，参数量仅为全量微调的0.78%，且较同规模随机基高出6.11个百分点；等价的“决策层基”无稳定迁移性。(3) 适配器式上岗不损伤源模态（Δ=0.00 pp），而全量微调虽在目标上最高，但以源模态灾难性退化为代价。(4) 马氏分数在严格源保持阈值下能高敏检测未见模态，提供实用的上岗触发信号；所有结果在三种随机种子上以配对自举置信区间报告。

Conclusion: 对未见模态的上线，必须触达卷积特征进行参数高效适配。在源模态上学得的低秩卷积基具备可迁移性：冻结基、仅训练上投影即可高效上岗，几乎不牺牲源模态性能。马氏分数可作为何时需要上岗的可靠检测器。这为实际部署提供了既稳健又经济的扩容策略。

Abstract: Deploying a medical imaging model that must later accommodate a modality it has never seen is a recurring practical problem: retraining the shared representation is expensive and destroys performance on the modalities already in service. We study this \emph{onboarding} problem under a strict leave-one-domain-out protocol, in which a convolutional backbone is pre-trained on source modalities (Kidney CT and Brain MRI), frozen permanently, and then required to accommodate an unseen modality (Chest X-ray). Under this protocol we establish three findings. First, decision-layer parameter-efficient fine-tuning is insufficient when the backbone has never observed the target modality: a linear probe and fully-connected LoRA both fall well short, whereas convolutional LoRA recovers most of the achievable accuracy, showing that adaptation must reach the convolutional features. Second, and centrally, the low-rank convolutional \emph{basis} learned on the source modalities \emph{transfers}: freezing that basis and training only its up-projections onboards the unseen modality using just $0.78\%$ of full fine-tuning's parameters, at an accuracy $6.11$ percentage points above a random basis of identical size, while an equivalent decision-layer basis exhibits no reliable transfer. Third, adapter-based onboarding leaves source-modality accuracy exactly unchanged ($Δ= 0.00$ pp), whereas full fine-tuning reaches the highest target accuracy only by catastrophically degrading the source modalities. A Mahalanobis score on frozen backbone features detects the unseen modality with high sensitivity at a strict source-retention threshold, providing a practical trigger for when onboarding is required. All results are reported over three seeds with paired bootstrap confidence intervals.

### [86] [Cross-Branch Conflict as a Shield: Safeguarding Facial Identities in Unified Multimodal Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16898)
*Weiwei Tan,Junxian Li,Rui Wang,Zhenhua Xu,Yanjun Zhang,Yu Leo Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CCS对抗防护框架，通过同时扰动UMM中的ViT理解分支与VAE生成分支并破坏二者特征兼容性，显著压制身份保持的图像编辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UMM具备强大的指令式人像编辑能力，带来隐私与滥用风险；现有针对理解或生成模型的单分支对抗保护在UMM上失效，因为UMM有多条互补视觉通路且融合会抵消单分支扰动。

Method: 对UMM统一编辑进行特征层面分析，发现ViT理解分支与VAE生成分支对同一图像存在结构一致性；单独扰动一条分支会在融合与生成阶段被削弱。基于此提出CCS：联合优化对抗扰动，(1) 让ViT与VAE各自的表示偏离干净表示；(2) 通过线性CKA显式最小化跨分支兼容性，制造不一致的视觉上下文，从而在多模态融合时无法恢复可靠身份信息。

Result: 在多种UMM与编辑场景上，CCS稳定优于现有防护方法，显著降低身份保持编辑的成功率，并在广泛实验中体现出一致性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 单分支扰动不足以破坏UMM统一编辑；通过同时削弱两条视觉通路并破坏其跨分支一致性的CCA式正则（基于线性CKA），可有效防止UMM在编辑中恢复身份信息，提供更强的一致对抗防护。

Abstract: Unified multimodal models (UMMs) have recently demonstrated powerful instruction-based image editing capabilities, but they also raise serious concerns about unauthorized manipulation of personal portraits. Existing adversarial protection methods are mainly designed for either visual understanding or image generation models and often become ineffective when transferred to UMMs, which process an image through multiple complementary visual pathways. In this work, we first conduct a feature-level analysis of unified image editing. We observe that the ViT-based understanding branch and the VAE-based generation branch exhibit non-trivial structural agreement for the same input image. Although perturbing an individual branch can reduce this agreement and induce intermediate hidden-state deviations, such effects are asymmetric and gradually attenuated during multimodal fusion and generation. These observations reveal that single-branch feature distortion is insufficient for consistently disrupting unified image editing. Motivated by this finding, we propose CCS, a unified adversarial protection framework that jointly drives the ViT and VAE representations away from their clean counterparts while explicitly disrupting their cross-branch compatibility through linear CKA. By simultaneously removing stable information from both visual pathways and creating incompatible visual contexts, CCS prevents the UMM from recovering reliable identity information during editing. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CCS consistently outperforms existing protection methods in suppressing identity-preserving edits.

### [88] [Splat-based 3D Scene Reconstruction with Extreme Motion-blur](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16926)
*Hyeonjoong Jang,Dongyoung Choi,Donggun Kim,Woohyun Kang,Min H. Kim*

TL;DR: 提出一种面向极端运动模糊场景的RGB-D高斯splat重建方法，联合位姿估计与去模糊，显著提升低光/快运动下的3D重建质量，并开源代码与数据集。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在高斯Splat框架中联合优化：1) 利用光流与ICP对齐连续RGB-D帧，初始化相对位姿与粗几何；2) 通过最小化与深度对齐的误差，调整3D高斯位置以细化相机位姿与几何；3) 建立曝光期间相机运动模型，渲染一系列清晰的中间帧，与模糊输入比较以进行去模糊与外观校正；4) 以RGB-D双模态监督，联合优化位姿、几何（高斯参数）与外观。

Result: 在作者构建的极端运动模糊RGB-D数据集上，较现有NeRF/高斯Splat与传统管线显著提升重建质量与位姿稳定性；能在快运动、低光下生成清晰纹理与准确几何。

Conclusion: 联合位姿估计与去模糊、并利用深度与高斯splat表示，可在极端模糊下实现高质量RGB-D 3D重建；对机器人建图、自动导航与AR具有应用价值，并提供公开代码与数据集。

Abstract: We propose a splat-based 3D scene reconstruction method from RGB-D input that effectively handles extreme motion blur, a frequent challenge in low-light environments. Under dim illumination, RGB frames often suffer from severe motion blur due to extended exposure times, causing traditional camera pose estimation methods, such as COLMAP, to fail. This results in inaccurate camera pose and blurry color input, compromising the quality of 3D reconstructions. Although recent 3D reconstruction techniques like Neural Radiance Fields and Gaussian Splatting have demonstrated impressive results, they rely on accurate camera trajectory estimation, which becomes challenging under fast motion or poor lighting conditions. Furthermore, rapid camera movement and the limited field of view of depth sensors reduce point cloud overlap, limiting the effectiveness of pose estimation with the ICP algorithm. To address these issues, we introduce a method that combines camera pose estimation and image deblurring using a Gaussian Splatting framework, leveraging both 3D Gaussian splats and depth inputs for enhanced scene representation. Our method first aligns consecutive RGB-D frames through optical flow and ICP, then refines camera poses and 3D geometry by adjusting Gaussian positions for optimal depth alignment. To handle motion blur, we model camera movement during exposure and deblur images by comparing the input with a series of sharp, rendered frames. Experiments on a new RGB-D dataset with extreme motion blur show that our method outperforms existing approaches, enabling high-quality reconstructions even in challenging conditions. This approach has broad implications for 3D mapping applications in robotics, autonomous navigation, and augmented reality. Both code and dataset are publicly available on https://github.com/KAIST-VCLAB/gs-extreme-motion-blur.

</details>

This approach provides a more effective and accurate solution for predicting bone age, which is critical in diagnosing pediatric endocrine diseases. This work uses two variations of the EfficientNet model (B0 and B4), where EfficientNetB4 is also finetuned with the Additive Attention mechanism. These three models predict the age for the original age, and their comparison is shown in curves. ### [90] [What Do They See? Interpreting Complex Road Scenarios Through the Eyes of Vision-Language-Action Models for Safe and Trustworthy Autonomous Vehicle Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16938)
*Kalpana Panda,Wesley Maia,Vinti Agarwal,Ross Greer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CVAA，通过生成式修复逐个移除前视相机图像中的检测目标，衡量对端到端自动驾驶规划/轨迹模型的因果影响；在nuScenes上构建Counter-nuScenes并用Alpamayo 1验证，发现车/行人沿路径影响最大，红灯影响相对面积不成比例，也暴露出对人类看来无关物体的过敏；进一步以机制可解释方法比较中间表示，连通行为审计与表征理解，提升可解释性与信任。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端自动驾驶模型在开放/闭环评测中表现良好，但其内部决策逻辑不透明，尤其在复杂交通场景中。需要一种方法区分场景中各对象对规划决策的因果作用，避免仅凭相关性解读，并将行为层面的审计连接到网络内部表征层面的理解。

Method: 提出Counterfactual Vision Action Analysis（CVAA）：对每个已检测到的对象，使用照片级生成式图像修复在前视相机图像中进行“反事实消融”，得到移除该对象的对照样本；将原/反事实图像输入相同端到端模型（Alpamayo 1），比较规划/轨迹输出差异以估计该对象的因果影响；进一步对原/修复图像对的中间层表示进行机制可解释性分析，跟踪各层受影响程度，探查模型是否以“对象为单位”编码。

Result: 在nuScenes的210个场景上构建了Counter-nuScenes数据集并实验：车辆与行人在模型路径附近对规划的因果影响占主导；交通信号灯虽在图像中占比小却影响显著；也发现模型会对人类认为无关的物体产生强烈响应，提示潜在脆弱性或偏差。

Conclusion: CVAA为端到端驾驶提供了从行为审计到表征理解的系统框架，可量化单个对象的因果作用并揭示内部表示的变化，有助于打造更可解释、更值得信赖的自动驾驶系统，同时发现并定位不合理的注意与偏差。

Abstract: End-to-end autonomous driving models are now able to navigate complex road scenarios, mapping raw sensor observations directly to observed paths for open-loop evaluation and often effective driving in closed-loop evaluation. Yet the internal logic of these safety-critical systems remains largely opaque, due to the complexity of traffic scenes. We propose a counterfactual ablation framework called Counterfactual Vision Action Analysis (CVAA) that systematically removes individual detected objects from front-camera images using photorealistic generative inpainting to prepare counterfactual sets to evaluate the difference in the model's response. This isolates the causal effect of each object's presence on the model's planning behaviour. Applied to the Alpamayo 1 trajectory predictor across 210 nuScenes driving scenes, we create a dataset Counter -nuScenes, using which we see that vehicles and pedestrians within the model's 'path' dominate causal influence as expected, while traffic lights, as expected, exert disproportionate effect relative to their image footprint. However, we also find cases where the model responds strongly to objects a human driver would consider irrelevant. This brings forth a deeper question: does the model itself view the scene as a sum of individual objects influencing the outcome, or does it encode an entirely different set of internal features that do not correspond to human-legible scene elements? To further understand this, we compare intermediate representations of original and inpainted image pairs using mechanistic interpretability techniques and examine the effect of the removal through the various model layers. Together, these two stages offer a path from behavioral auditing to representational understanding, creating explainable driving systems and solidifying human-AI trust.

### [91] [When Physical Preferences Meet Semantic Constraints: Physical and Semantic Direct Preference Optimization for Text-to-Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16947)
*Siwei Meng,Yawei Luo,Shu Zhang,Ping Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 他们提出PSDPO，在保持语义一致性的同时提升T2V生成的物理合理性，通过在DPO框架内按物理与语义一致度重加权偏好对，抑制“物理-语义冲突”，理论上界语义漂移并用分阶段优化进一步降低漂移，实验在VideoPhy-2上物理性最高提升约2倍且VBench语义保持强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有T2V偏好学习常仅比较两视频的物理动态优劣，却不管是否符合文本语义，导致优化朝“物理更好但语义跑偏”的方向，系统性产生物理-语义冲突，需要一种在优化时同时考虑物理与语义信号的一致性的机制。

Method: 将问题表述为受约束的偏好优化：在标准DPO中对每个偏好对引入基于“物理评分”和“语义一致性”的调制因子，仅当两者信号一致时放大梯度，冲突时抑制；给出梯度级分析，证明该重加权能将由冲突对引发的语义漂移限制在可控残差内；进一步提出分阶段（staged）训练协议以逐步减少累计漂移；全方法保持在常规DPO框架内，无需额外模型或损失项。

Result: 在VideoPhy-2基准上物理合理性相较基线最高提升约2倍；在VBench上维持强语义一致性，相比既有偏好方法在物理与语义之间取得更稳健平衡。

Conclusion: 通过PSDPO在不引入额外模型的情况下，于DPO内实现对冲突偏好的自适应抑制，并配合分阶段训练有效控制语义漂移，在提升视频物理性同时保持语义忠实，优于现有偏好学习方案。

Abstract: Text-to-video (T2V) generation models have achieved strong visual realism, but improving physical plausibility can come at the cost of semantic consistency with the input text. This tension arises because physical preference is typically determined by comparing dynamics between two videos, without accounting for whether either video faithfully depicts the scene specified by the prompt, making physical-semantic conflict a systematic tendency under this supervision paradigm. We formulate this challenge as a constrained preference optimization problem and propose Physical and Semantic Direct Preference Optimization (PSDPO), which modulates each preference pair's contribution based on the agreement between its physical and semantic signals. A gradient-level analysis shows that PSDPO bounds the semantic drift from conflicting pairs to a controllable residual, and further motivates a staged optimization protocol that provably reduces cumulative drift. The resulting method operates entirely within the standard DPO framework, requiring no auxiliary models or additional loss terms. Experiments show that PSDPO improves physical plausibility by up to $2\times$ over the baseline on VideoPhy-2, while maintaining strong semantic consistency on VBench, achieving a more reliable balance than existing preference-based methods.

### [93] [EvoGUI: An Evolution-Aware Benchmark for GUI State-Transition Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17050)
*Yaohan Yang,Minglei Shi,Borui Zhang,Jie Zhou,Jiwen Lu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EvoGUI 提出一套将规范化 GUI 轨迹转为三类 VQA 诊断任务的框架（时序排序、逆向动作/数值预测、对比式一步后继判别），构建了跨 120 个域的 EvoGUI-Bench，并显示当前多模态模型在状态转移理解上仍有显著差距（最强仅 60.4 EvoGain）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端 GUI 代理的成功率混合了感知、语义落地、规划与容错等多因素，难以单独诊断模型“动作如何改变界面状态”的能力。需要一个可扩展、免额外标注、专注于状态转移理解的评测方法。

Method: 将已规范化的 GUI 交互轨迹自动转化为三类 VQA 探针：1) 时间顺序判定（推断界面变化的先后）；2) 逆向动作/值预测（从状态变化反推采取的动作或填入的值）；3) 对比式一步后继判别（区分真实下一步界面与干扰项）。标签直接来源于轨迹顺序与日志化动作，无需额外注释。基于 Mind2Web 与 WebLINX 构建 EvoGUI-Bench（3,000 样例/120 域），对 28 个视觉-语言模型进行零样本评测，并以“EvoGain”指标汇总表现。

Conclusion: EvoGUI-Bench 为 GUI 代理评估提供了可扩展的诊断补充，能隔离并量化“状态转移理解”能力；现有模型在该维度存在大量提升空间，提示需要针对性表征与学习方法。

Abstract: GUI agents must reason about how actions transform interface states, but end-to-end success rates entangle this ability with perception, grounding, planning, and recovery. We introduce EvoGUI, a diagnostic framework that converts normalized GUI trajectories into three complementary visual question answering probes: temporal ordering, inverse action/value prediction, and contrastive one-step successor discrimination. Their labels are derived from trajectory order and logged actions, requiring no additional task-label annotation after trajectory normalization. We instantiate EvoGUI-Bench from Mind2Web and WebLINX, yielding 3,000 instances across 120 domains, and evaluate 28 vision-language model configurations zero-shot. The strongest model reaches only 60.4 EvoGain, while model scale and GUI specialization do not reliably predict performance. These results establish EvoGUI-Bench as a scalable diagnostic complement to end-to-end GUI-agent evaluation while exposing substantial headroom in state-transition understanding. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/Yyhhh6/EvoGUI.

### [94] [Searching for Task-Specific Vision Paths: Evolutionary Block Pruning Across Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17052)
*Tarun Tomar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 研究在不微调情况下，固定预算下可跳过哪些视觉编码器块，以加速/省算而尽量不掉点。提出共享K块路径与基于能力标签的K块路径，并用源平衡进化搜索找最优跳块组合；在多模型、多数据上验证，搜索结果可跨架构迁移，但能力专化路径的可迁移性不稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态视觉-语言模型对不同问题（OCR、计数、目标、属性、空间关系）一律跑完整视觉编码器，计算冗余。希望在不重新训练的前提下，通过选择性跳过部分视觉块，在给定算力预算下维持或提升任务表现。

Method: 提出两种策略：1) 共享K块路径：为所有问题统一跳过同一组K个视觉块；2) 能力特定K块策略：基于已知能力标签（如OCR等）为每类选择同规模但可能不同的跳块集。为搜索最优跳块组合，引入源平衡进化搜索，并与独立排名、连续移除、随机路径在相同预算下对比。实验在Qwen2.5-VL-3B-Instruct、SmolVLM2-2.2B-Instruct，以及876例图像互斥的选择集上进行，并测试跨架构迁移。

Result: 跨架构可迁移：在SmolVLM2上，来自搜索的“共享4块路径”较独立构造提升4.91个百分点。能力专化不稳定：在Qwen上，6块能力策略较共享路径提升2.17点（主要因OCR提升7.10点）；但在封闭IIIT5K上，SmolVLM2的OCR专用路径比其共享路径低13.6点。

Conclusion: 组合式搜索能稳定优于简单或随机的路径构造，并可在一定程度上跨模型迁移；但基于能力标签的专用视觉路径缺乏普适可迁移性，不应被视为通用方案。

Abstract: Vision-language models normally execute the same complete vision encoder for every question, even when OCR, counting, object, attribute, and spatial queries may not require identical computation. We study whether fixed-budget combinations of vision blocks can be skipped without fine-tuning. A shared K-block route skips one searched set of exactly K blocks for every question, while a capability-specific K-block policy selects one same-size route using a known capability label. We introduce a source-balanced evolutionary search and compare it with independent ranking, contiguous removal, and random routes at matched budgets. Experiments use Qwen2.5-VL-3B-Instruct, SmolVLM2-2.2B-Instruct, and an 876-example image-disjoint selection split. Search transfers across architectures: on SmolVLM2, the searched shared four-block route beats independent construction by 4.91 percentage points. Capability specialization is less stable. On Qwen, the six-block capability policy beats the shared route by 2.17 points, driven by a 7.10-point OCR gain. On sealed IIIT5K, however, the SmolVLM2 OCR-specific route trails its shared route by 13.6 points. Combinatorial search reliably improves route construction, but capability labels do not define universally transferable vision pathways.

### [95] [High-Capacity Robust Watermarking Technology for High-Resolution Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17056)
*Shaowu Wu,Wei Lu,Qing Qian,Mingsen Deng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种面向高分辨率图像（1024×1024）的高容量鲁棒水印方法，可嵌入4KB（32768比特），达到0.0313 bpp；采用分块嵌入、对称可逆卷积/反卷积编码器-解码器、全局与局部加权损失，并在多种攻击下保持较强鲁棒与良好不可感知性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有水印多针对低分辨率图像，容量固定且偏小（30/100/256比特等），难以满足实际对高分辨率、可扩容量与鲁棒性的需求。

Method: - 分块（block-wise）策略：在局部区域嵌入水印，便于在资源受限下训练并提升局部鲁棒与质量控制。
- 编码器/解码器：三层卷积与三层反卷积构成的可逆对称结构，确保水印与图像特征耦合/解耦一致性。
- 损失设计：结合全局与局部损失并加权，约束局部块的视觉质量与鲁棒性，从而提升整体不可感知与鲁棒性。

Result: 在1024×1024图像中成功嵌入4KB水印（0.0313 bpp），大量实验显示在多种噪声攻击下保持较强鲁棒，同时视觉质量良好。

Conclusion: 该方法在高分辨率场景下实现高容量、强鲁棒、较好不可感知的图像水印，分块训练与对称可逆结构及全局-局部加权损失是关键。

Abstract: Most existing watermarking techniques are primarily designed for low-resolution images, with few methods tailored for high-resolution images. Moreover, the embedding capacity is often limited to fixed lengths (e.g., 30, 100, 256 bits, etc.), which struggles to meet practical demands. To address these issues, this paper proposes a high-capacity robust watermarking method for high-resolution images, capable of embedding a watermark of 4 KB (32,768 bits) into images with a resolution of 1024*1024, achieving an embedding rate of 0.0313 bpp. Specifically, this paper adopts a block-wise strategy to effectively embed the watermark into local regions, enabling the network to train and learn normally even under low-resource conditions. The encoder and decoder structures respectively employ a reversible symmetric architecture with three convolutional and three deconvolutional layers, ensuring consistency in the coupling and decoupling of the watermark and image features. Additionally, the loss function combines global and local losses with weighted contributions. By incorporating constraints on the visual quality and robustness of local block regions, the overall imperceptibility and robustness of the image are further enhanced. Extensive experimental results verify that the proposed method is effective and feasible in high-resolution image scenarios with high-capacity watermarking, while demonstrating strong robustness against various noise attacks.

</details>


### [96] [AdvSerial: Physical Adversarial Attacks on Infrastructure-mounted Pedestrian Detectors via Semantic Feature Suppression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17069)
*Yuanhao Huang,Yilong Ren,Jinlei Wang,Xuesong Bai,Jinchuan Zhang,Haiyang Yu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AdvSerial：面向基础设施高角度监控场景的物理连续对抗贴片生成框架，通过2D-3D联合优化与时序一致性约束，在多种行人检测器上实现高成功率且具迁移性，暴露出监控系统在时域与3D视角下的持续失效模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基础设施监控（路侧/高速/智慧城市）广泛采用视觉行人检测，但物理对抗攻击会导致关键安防/交通系统可靠性下降。现有方法多聚焦单帧、低角度、或忽视3D与时间一致性，难以在真实高角度摄像与连续视频下稳定失效。作者希望构建能在物理世界、跨帧连续、跨模型迁移、且在高角度监控条件下有效的攻击方法，以揭示系统脆弱性并推动防御研究。

Conclusion: AdvSerial在高角度基础设施监控下实现连续物理对抗，兼具时序一致与跨模型迁移，并对现有补丁检测与3D时序感知具韧性。结果表明需要面向运动与3D感知的综合防御，以提升关键基础设施视觉系统的安全可靠性。

Abstract: AI-based visual perception systems are increasingly deployed in infrastructure surveillance, including roadside monitoring units, highway cameras, and smart-city pedestrian management systems. The security vulnerability of these systems to physical adversarial attacks poses a direct threat to the reliable operation of transportation infrastructure. We propose AdvSerial, a dynamic 2D--3D joint optimization framework for generating continuous high-angle physical adversarial patches against pedestrian detectors in infrastructure-based scenarios. We UV-map a boundary-aware quilted texture onto 3D garments, combine 2D digital attacks with 3D sparse- and continuous-frame rendering, and explicitly suppress person-specific semantic features while enforcing temporal continuity. A Feature Smooth Quilting strategy reduces visible patch boundaries and bounds cross-seam feature discontinuities. A serial-frame loss encourages long uninterrupted sequences of detection failures. In physical world experiments, AdvSerial achieves a 74.8% attack success rate on YOLO-v5 and degrades mean detection confidence from 84.30% to 39.38%. Experiments spanning eight detectors with different architectures demonstrate strong transferability. Notably, it achieves an $89.71%$ attack success rate on YOLO-v2 and resists both patch-detection defenses (NapGuard) and 3D-temporal perception (Sparse4D-v3). The results reveal persistent, temporally consistent failure modes under high-angle surveillance, and motivate the design of motion-aware and 3D-aware defenses for security-critical infrastructure deployments.

### [97] [ALLUDE: A Unified Evaluation System for Configurable Attacks in Differentiable Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17077)
*Mansi Phute,Alexander Greenhalgh,Matthew Hull,Haoran Wang,Alec Helbling,ShengYun Peng,Elliott Faa,Willian Lunardi,Martin Andreoni,Wenke Lee,Duen Horng Chau*

TL;DR: ALLUDE 提供一个跨平台、可微渲染驱动的统一评测系统，用于在多场景、多气象、多相机轨迹与多检测模型下系统地评估和优化对抗攻击；结果显示现有攻击在更现实、连续条件下显著退化。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 ALLUDE：基于可微渲染的跨平台（Linux/Windows）统一评测与优化系统。设计丰富的可配置维度（场景-物体组合、天气、优化器、相机轨迹、检测模型）。采用两阶段评测：1) 使用拉丁超立方采样从5400种配置中抽取具有代表性的子集进行广覆盖评测；2) 在多样天气与连续相机轨迹下对现有攻击（CAMOU、RAUCA、FCA）进行压力测试。系统支持端到端可微渲染以在变化的部署条件下直接优化攻击。

Result: 在广泛配置下的系统性实验显示：所有现有攻击在多变天气与连续相机运动下的成功率均下降，揭示了此前工作评测不足与攻击鲁棒性不足。ALLUDE 展示了在多检测模型与复杂条件下的覆盖能力，并能在可微渲染回路中适配环境变化进行优化。

Conclusion: ALLUDE 填补了对抗攻击评测生态的空白，提供统一、可扩展、跨平台且端到端可微的评测与优化框架。其实验表明现有攻击在更真实设定下性能退化，强调今后需在多样环境与动态条件下设计与评估更稳健的对抗方法；代码开源，便于社区复现与扩展。

Abstract: Adversarial attacks against vision models like object detectors are often evaluated under limited conditions, leaving their performance under-characterized. Bridging simulation and differentiable rendering enables more robust, end-to-end evaluation of these adversarial attacks, yet there is no easy-to-use, unified system that offers a rich set of customizable configurations for adversarial attacks across multiple scenes, objects, environmental and lighting conditions, and camera trajectories. We present ALLUDE, which addresses these gaps, offering first-of-its-kind evaluation capabilities across Linux and Windows. We comprehensively demonstrate ALLUDE's evaluation breadth through a two-pronged strategy: (1) using Latin Hypercube Sampling, we draw a representative subset from 5,400 configurations spanning 10 scene-object pairs, 9 weather conditions, 4 optimizers, 5 camera trajectories, and 3 detection models; (2) we stress-test existing attacks (CAMOU, RAUCA, FCA) under diverse weather conditions and continuous camera trajectories, revealing degradation of attack success across every attack, exposing evaluation gaps in prior work. Through ALLUDE's end-to-end differentiable rendering, adversarial attacks can be optimized against shifting real-world deployment conditions. Our cross-platform code is open source.

Abstract: Generative CAD modeling has broad design and application potential. We present ParaCAD, an autoregressive framework for point-cloud-conditioned B-Rep generation that directly operates on native parametric surfaces. ParaCAD introduces a surface-centric tokenization that explicitly encodes each face by its exact surface type and continuous parameters, preserving the intrinsic semantics of CAD geometry. Our model first generates parametric surfaces with constrained UV domains, and then constructs a valid B-Rep by globally intersecting these surfaces to recover edges and vertices. ParaCAD places point-cloud-conditioned generation at the core of B-Rep synthesis, making it practical for user-guided reconstruction and seamless integration into existing 3D generation pipelines. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ParaCAD produces accurate B-Reps with faithful point-cloud alignment, outperforming point-based baselines in geometric precision, robustness, watertightness and downstream usability.

### [99] [HarmoHOI: Harmonizing Appearance and 3D Motion for Multi-view Hand-Object Interaction Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17097)
*Lingwei Dang,Juntong Li,Zonghan Li,Hongwen Zhang,Liang An,Wei Min,Yebin Liu,Qingyao Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HarmoHOI提出一个统一扩散框架，同时生成多视角一致的手-物交互视频与全局对齐的3D点轨迹，解决复杂手部动作与遮挡下的几何与外观一致性难题，并达成SOTA视觉质量、运动合理性与几何一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频基础模型虽有强先验，但在多视角HOI合成上易因手部复杂运动与遮挡而失去一致性；缺乏多视数据也限制了模型训练与泛化。作者认为实现稳健的多视一致性必须依赖全局对齐的3D几何与运动。

Method: 提出HarmoHOI：1) 混合多视扩散Transformer（Mixture of Multi-view Diffusion Transformer），把RGB视频与3D点轨共同建模；将3D点轨表示为“伪视频”，嵌入与2D潜空间对齐以缩小域差；2) 全局运动对齐扩散（Global Motion Aligning Diffusion），将粗糙点轨细化为度量尺度、全局对齐的3D轨迹；3) 在扩散去噪中实现2D外观与3D运动的协同演化；4) 采用混合数据课程学习，将单视先验迁移到同步多视生成以缓解数据稀缺。

Conclusion: 将3D几何与运动作为一等公民融入扩散生成，可显著提升多视HOI合成的一致性与真实性；通过伪视频表示与全局运动对齐扩散，实现2D-3D协同建模，并可用课程学习从单视到多视高效迁移。

Abstract: Hand-Object Interaction (HOI) synthesis is a cornerstone for animation production and embodied AI. Despite the strong priors of video foundation models, multi-view consistent HOI synthesis remains challenging due to complex hand motions and occlusions. We present HarmoHOI, a unified diffusion framework that jointly and harmoniously generates synchronized multi-view HOI videos and globally aligned 3D point tracks. Our core insight is that robust multi-view consistency fundamentally requires globally aligned 3D geometry and motion. To this end, we propose a Mixture of Multi-view Diffusion Transformer that co-models RGB videos and 3D point tracks. By representing point tracks as pseudo-videos, we align 3D geometric signals with the 2D latent space of foundation models, thereby minimizing the domain gap and easing adaptation of priors. To further ensure geometry consistency, we introduce Global Motion Aligning Diffusion, which refines coarse point tracks into metric-scale, globally aligned 3D trajectories. HarmoHOI enables on-the-fly co-evolution of 2D appearance and 3D motion during denoising. To overcome the scarcity of multi-view HOI data, we employ a hybrid data curriculum learning strategy that successfully transfers generic priors from single-view data to synchronized multi-view generation. Experimental results show that HarmoHOI achieves state-of-the-art performance in visual quality, motion plausibility, and multi-view geometric consistency. Project page available at https://droliven.github.io/HarmoHOI_project.

### [100] [DepthART: Scaling Foundation Monocular Depth to Tiny Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17099)
*Feng Xue,Wu Chen,Mingshuai Zhao,Guofeng Zhong,Anlong Ming,Haozhe Wang,Dianqiao Lei,Zhaowen Lin,Haiyang Zhang,Nicu Sebe*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DepthART 提出面向端侧的微小型单目深度估计模型，通过抗偏置数据采样与相机条件化微调，在保持跨数据集泛化的同时稳定进行度量尺度适配，显著超越以往tiny基线，速度与准确度兼顾，并在多种硬件上实现高FPS。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 几何大模型在单目深度的跨场景与度量尺度上已显著进步，但这些收益难以迁移到tiny模型：小模型易过拟合数据集偏置，且在相机变化下进行全量微调会破坏可迁移几何，导致度量尺度不稳。亟需一种兼顾泛化、度量稳定与端侧效率的tiny方案。

Method: 1) 偏置鲁棒的数据采样：在相同训练预算下，通过更均衡/多样的样本选择，降低数据集分布偏置带来的过拟合。2) 相机条件化微调：蒸馏得到的编码器冻结，仅对与相机内参相关的尺度/映射进行条件化调整，实现在相机切换时的稳定度量自适应，并保留跨数据集可迁移几何。提供可扩展的模型族以适配不同算力。

Result: 在多数据集上，DepthART 在零样本泛化与度量精度上均优于既有tiny基线；举例：在 NYUD v2 上，DepthART-S 零样本 δ1=0.964。一些场景下接近重型模型表现。推理速度：RTX A6000 严格FP32下224^2/448^2分别达347/245 FPS；Orin NX 8GB TF32达102 FPS；Jetson Nano 4GB FP32超过15 FPS。

Conclusion: 通过针对小模型容量瓶颈的两项简单策略，DepthART 在不增加训练预算的情况下实现更强的跨域泛化与稳定的度量适配，并以极高效率适配多种端侧硬件，为实用化单目深度估计提供紧凑而可扩展的方案。

Abstract: Recent geometric foundation models (e.g., Metric3D, Depth Anything and UniDepth) have substantially improved monocular depth estimation (MDE) in both cross-scene generalization and metric-scale prediction, yet these gains have not translated to tiny models. We bridge this gap with DepthART (Depth Anything Rethought for Tiny Models), which is a compact MDE model for on-device deployment across diverse scenes. We first identify two capacity-driven bottlenecks in tiny models: (i) overfitting to dataset-specific distribution bias and (ii) unstable metric adaptation under camera shift, where full fine-tuning easily damages transferable geometry. Accordingly, DepthART combines two simple but effective strategies: a bias-resistant data sampling scheme to reduce distribution bias under the same training budget, and a camera-conditioned fine-tuning protocol that freezes the distilled encoder and adjusts metric scale conditioned on intrinsics while better preserving cross-dataset generalization. Across datasets, DepthART consistently surpasses previous tiny baselines in both zero-shot generalization and metric accuracy (e.g., zero-shot $δ_1$=0.964 for DepthART-S on NYUD v2), and in some cases approaches heavy models. We further provide a scalable model family, with DepthART-S reaching 347/245 FPS (strict FP32) on an RTX A6000 at $224^2/448^2$, 102 FPS (TF32) on a Orin NX 8GB, and over 15 FPS (FP32) on a Jetson Nano 4GB.

### [101] [The generator is the tracker: Multi-object tracking by painting persistent identity colours](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17120)
*Haiyu Yang,Miel Hostens*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 作者将MOT从“检测+关联”的外部状态范式，改为用生成式视频扩散模型在像素中直接维护身份：同色=同人。通过微调22B文本转视频模型并用链式窗口生成，使ID颜色在长视频中持续。结果在DanceTrack上HOTA 40.3，关联分数优异、检测薄弱；同样窗口若用传统后处理关联仅18.2 HOTA。生成器可在遮挡后以42%条件概率重获身份，超出外观嵌入基线（0）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战传统MOT必须显式维护身份（轨迹缓冲、运动模型、外观特征）的假设，探索强生成模型能否把“身份”内化到像素生成过程，实现无需检测器和跟踪堆栈的端到端跟踪。

Method: 对大型文本转视频扩散模型（LTX-2.3，22B）进行轻量LoRA微调，使其把RGB片段翻译为“ID-map”视频：每个人以独立纯色表示，颜色随时间保持。长序列用链式窗口生成，每个窗口条件于前一窗口的干净尾部；再进行短暂续写微调，使模型学会延展已有着色，实现跨窗口的身份延续，无需显式跟踪、运动或ReID模块。

Result: 在DanceTrack测试服上取得HOTA 40.3。尽管低于SOTA（≥70），但关联分（AssA 44.1）超过基准套件所有传统跟踪器，主要短板在检测。对照实验显示：把同样生成窗口交给经典后处理关联仅18.2 HOTA；逐帧IoU关联会碎片化轨迹，而生成颜色保持完整。对383个挖掘的遮挡事件，模型在超出其时间上下文的间隙后仍能以42%条件率重新找回身份，外观嵌入基线为0，表明颜色分配是涌现的ReID信号。

Conclusion: 生成式“在像素中维护身份”的思路可行，能在关联上优于传统管线，但受限于检测能力。链式生成与续写微调是关键机制，并在遮挡后显示再识别能力。未来需提升检测/召回或与检测器结合，以弥补短板。

Abstract: Multi-object tracking (MOT) is conventionally decomposed into detection followed by association, with object identity maintained as external state: track buffers, motion models, and appearance embeddings. We ask whether a video generator can maintain that state in pixels. We fine-tune a 22B text-to-video diffusion model (LTX-2.3) with a lightweight in-context LoRA to translate an RGB clip into an ID-map clip, a video in which every person is painted a flat, distinct color that persists over time: same color, same identity. Long videos are generated as chained windows, where each window is conditioned on the cleaned tail of the previous one. A brief continuation fine-tune teaches the model to extend a given coloring, after which identity flows through the chain with no tracker, no motion model, and no re-identification module. On the DanceTrack test server, our system, to our knowledge the first generative tracker evaluated there and the only entry with no detector and no tracking stack, reaches 40.3 HOTA. This is well below today's specialist state of the art (>=70 HOTA), but with a unique, inverted error profile: its association score (AssA 44.1) exceeds every tracker of the original benchmark suite while detection remains the sole deficit. Controlled comparisons show the mechanism matters: the same generated windows linked by classical post-hoc association score 2x worse (18.2 HOTA), and frame-to-frame IoU association fragments tracks that the generator's colors keep whole. On 383 mined occlusion events, the generator re-acquires identities after gaps at a 42% conditional rate where appearance-embedding baselines score zero, including gaps longer than its temporal context, evidence that the generator's color assignment functions as an emergent re-identification signal. We release code, checkpoints, and the full pre-registered experimental log.

</details>


### [102] [Learning Emotion from Motion: Kinetic Multi-Stream Skeleton Modeling with Metadata-Conditioned Weak Label Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17121)
*Sosuke Suzuki,Yijin Wei,Koichiro Kamide,Ran Dong,Haoran Xie,Chao Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一个多分支骨架动作情绪识别框架，通过6D旋转分支、部件感知的多流运动分支和基于元数据的弱标签分布学习分支，独立训练并在推理时概率级融合，相比旋转基线显著提升准确率与Macro-F1，并表明速度/骨骼流与手臂/腿部区域是关键线索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 情绪由细微、关系性的身体运动体现，硬标签难以表达类别间模糊性；现有基于骨架的方法对这些动态关系与不确定性建模不足，需要更鲁棒且可解释的方案以应对挑战赛DIEM-A任务。

Method: 设计三分支：1）6D旋转分支，稳健编码关节朝向；2）部件感知的多流运动分支，包含位置、速度、骨骼等流并按身体部位建模；3）元数据条件的弱标签分布学习分支，用元数据调节软标签分布以刻画类别不确定性。三分支独立训练，推理阶段进行概率级集成。并进行可解释性消融，评估不同流与部位的重要性。

Result: 在10折留演员交叉验证下，相比旋转基线，准确率从0.271提升到0.366，Macro-F1从0.252提升到0.353。消融表明速度流与骨骼流、以及手臂与腿部区域对情绪识别贡献显著。

Conclusion: 多分支融合与弱标签分布学习有效捕捉细微和不确定的情绪运动线索，显著优于基线；关键线索来自速度/骨骼动力学与四肢部位。框架具备可解释性，为情绪动作识别提供实用范式。

Abstract: Skeleton-based emotion recognition from body motion remains challenging because emotional expressions are often characterized by subtle dynamic and relational motion cues, and hard labels may not fully capture ambiguity among related emotion categories. For the DIEM-A task in the MMAC ACII 2026 Challenge, we propose a multi-branch skeleton-based emotion recognition framework that combines a 6D rotation-based branch, a part-aware kinetic multi-stream branch, and a metadata-conditioned weak label distribution learning (LDL) branch. The branches are trained independently and fused by a probability-level ensemble at inference time. In 10-fold leave-performer-out cross-validation, the proposed framework improves Accuracy from 0.271 to 0.366 and Macro-F1 from 0.252 to 0.353 over the rotation-based baseline. Explainability ablations show that velocity and bone streams, as well as arm and leg regions, provide important cues for recognizing emotional body motion.

</details>


### [103] [Denoising Models Develop Human-Like Perceptual Illusion Representations Across Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17138)
*Gautam Ranka,Paras Chopra*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文发现去噪视觉模型在内部层面编码了亮度错觉，但这些表征不会体现在输出像素上，被称为“知觉幽灵”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明，训练于自然图像的深度网络在亮度错觉任务上的输出与人类一致，但证据几乎都来自输出层面，尚不清楚模型内部是否、在哪里以及如何表示这些错觉。

Method: 以多种去噪架构为对象：1) 在不同层与通道上检测能区分“错觉区 vs 物理匹配对照区”的表征；2) 比较去噪目标与架构对该效应的贡献；3) 用经心理物理验证的FLODOG模型相关（Spearman ρ≥0.70）与参数化强度梯度，检验内部激活是否随错觉强度单调变化；4) 通道消融以因果验证这些通道对内部信号的特异性与重要性；5) 将这些表征注入生成流程，评估是否产生可测像素变化。

Result: 在特定中间层出现对错觉敏感的通道，能有效区分错觉与对照；去噪目标比架构选择更关键；这些通道的激活与FLODOG强相关并随错觉强度单调变化；消融这些通道显著改变内部信号；但将该表征注入生成并不引起任何可测像素改变，跨架构一致。

Conclusion: 去噪模型内部存在与人类亮度知觉一致的“错觉敏感”表征，但它们对最终输出不可见，构成“知觉幽灵”。这是在视觉去噪模型中首次对感知表征与输出解耦的系统性刻画，提示训练目标比架构更决定此类内部表征。

Abstract: Deep neural networks trained on natural images are shown to produce outputs consistent with human observers for brightness illusions. While this phenomenon has been documented across architectures, all evidence, to date, is measured at the output level: restored pixels, decoded trajectories, or classification decisions. Whether these models actually represent illusions internally, and if so where and how, remains unknown. We show that denoising models develop illusion-sensitive representations at specific internal layers, across varied architectures. Specifically, we identify the layers and channels that discriminate illusory from physically matched control regions. We show that the denoising objective is a more important driver of the effect than the architecture. On domain-appropriate stimuli, these activations track a validated psychophysical model of human brightness perception (FLODOG; Spearman $ρ\geq 0.70$) and scale monotonically with parametric illusion strength. Leveraging these findings, we provide causal evidence via channel ablation showing that illusion-sensitive channels specifically and substantially affect the internal signal. Yet injecting these representations into the generation pipeline produces no measurable pixel shift across all tested architectures; we term such representations perceptual phantoms: active in internal processing yet invisible to any output-based evaluation. While related internal-output dissociations have been characterized in language models, this is the first such characterization for perceptual representations in denoising vision models.

### [104] [STBridge: Shared-Target Alignment for Bridging Understanding and Generation in UMMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17140)
*Ye Wang,Hongjun Wang,Hao Fang,Tongyuan Bai,Zuwei Long,Peixian Chen,Wei Liu,Weibo Gu,Xing Sun,Rui Ma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出当前统一多模态模型（UMMs）在“理解-生成”之间存在显著对齐缺口：文字描述与图像编辑结果常不一致。为此提出STBridge，通过共享“目标状态”将文本理解与图像生成贯通，并采用“先对齐、后优化”的策略（SFT+顺序RL）提升一致性，在多项基准上取得一致改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仅靠统一架构并不能保证语义一致性。UMM在图像编辑中可能正确描述目标却生成不一致的编辑，说明理解输出（语言）与生成输出（视觉）受不同空间与流程约束，缺乏共同的目标语义纽带，需要一种机制让二者围绕同一“目标状态”协同。

Method: 提出STBridge的共享目标对齐框架：以指令定义目标状态，模型先产生目标caption（目标表达），再据此执行图像编辑（目标实现），以共享信息流替代分离的任务路径。训练采用两阶段：1) 监督微调建立共享目标通道；2) 顺序式强化学习进一步优化围绕目标的协同与一致性。并设计对齐评估，比较模型生成的目标caption与编辑后图像的一致性。

Result: 实证显示：现有UMMs在细粒度实体、属性、空间关系、局部细节方面对齐较弱；STBridge在视觉理解、图像生成、图像编辑基准上均优于初始化模型；对齐分析表明其显著缩小了描述与生成之间的差距。

Conclusion: 语义统一不能仅凭架构实现；通过共享目标状态并以SFT+RL进行后训练，能有效弥合UMM的理解-生成对齐缺口。STBridge提供了一条通用且可迁移的后训练策略，提升跨模态一致性与编辑质量。

Abstract: Unified multimodal models (UMMs) aim to integrate visual understanding and generation within a single architecture, but architectural unification alone does not ensure semantic consistency. A model may describe the intended target correctly while generating an inconsistent edit. This exposes an understanding-generation alignment gap: linguistic and visual outputs live in different spaces, yet should be governed by the same target semantics. We study this gap in image editing, where an instruction defines a target state that can be both described and visually realized. Given a source image and an edit instruction, we compare a UMM's target caption with its edited image to test whether the two outputs converge on the same result. Our analysis shows that existing UMMs remain weakly aligned, especially for fine-grained entities, attributes, spatial relations, and local details, indicating that semantic unification is not achieved by architecture alone. To bridge this gap, we propose STBridge, a shared-target alignment framework that connects understanding and generation through a common target state. Here the target caption expresses the desired visual result, while the edited image realizes it visually, replacing separate task-specific paths with a shared information flow from target expression to target realization. STBridge follows an align-then-optimize strategy: supervised fine-tuning first establishes the shared-target channel, and sequential reinforcement learning further refines target-centered coordination. Across visual understanding, image generation, and image editing benchmarks, STBridge consistently improves over the initialization model. Alignment analysis confirms that STBridge narrows the gap between what the model describes and what it generates, demonstrating shared-target alignment as an effective post-training strategy for bridging understanding and generation in UMMs.

### [105] [Noise-Robust Box-Supervised Infrared Small Target Detection via Physics-Inspired Soft Label Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17148)
*Xizhe Zhang,Fan Shi,Mianzhao Wang,Jiangpeng Zheng,Xu Cheng,Shengyong Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 像素级掩码标注成本高且不确定（边界模糊、纹理弱），而仅用框监督会被背景污染，如何从“被污染的框”稳定地产生有效的像素级监督是核心难题。

Method: 提出Hotspot-Anchored Label Optimization (HALO)：在每个框内基于局部背景统计定位辐射学热点锚点；以此为中心合成物理锚定高斯(PAG)软标签，离线生成连续像素级软监督；与检测器骨干解耦，无需在线更新标签。

Result: 在公共数据集与标准紧框下，HALO与代表性框监督方法性能相当；在更贴近实际的松散或偏移框标注下显著更鲁棒，且对不同骨干网络保持一致表现。

Conclusion: HALO能将嘈杂框监督稳定转化为物理一致的软标签，改善红外小目标检测在不精确标注情形下的鲁棒性；并通过污染感知的工作区间分析揭示内在信杂比与性能的关系。

Abstract: Infrared small target detection (IRSTD) commonly relies on pixel-level mask supervision. Such annotations, however, are costly and inherently uncertain because infrared targets have blurred boundaries and weak textures. We formulate box-supervised IRSTD as a problem distinct from generic box-to-mask segmentation and point-supervised IRSTD. Its central challenge is to construct stable pixel-level soft supervision from highly contaminated boxes. To this end, we propose Hotspot-Anchored Label Optimization (HALO). HALO localizes a radiometric anchor inside each box under local background-statistics constraints, then synthesizes a Physically Anchored Gaussian (PAG) soft label around the anchor. This turns noisy box supervision into continuous, pixel-level soft labels. The entire process is performed offline before training, remains decoupled from the detector backbone, and requires no online label updates. Experiments on public datasets show that HALO is competitive with representative box-supervised methods under standard tight boxes. Under looser or shifted box annotations that better approximate real scenarios, HALO is substantially more robust while remaining consistent across backbones. We further introduce a contamination-aware operating-regime analysis to characterize the effective boundary of this class of methods and reveal how intrinsic signal-to-clutter ratio relates to performance.

### [106] [VLA-ReID: Video-Level Association for Re-Identification in Multi-Object Tracking with Highly Similar Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17157)
*Yanrong Qin,Xiaoyan Cao,Yao Yao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出VLA-ReID与FCAE+CAS，面向蜂群等高密度小目标场景，通过视频级全局关联训练与共同外观抑制，缓解训练-推理不匹配并放大细小差异，在BEE24上显著减少ID切换并全面提升HOTA/MOTA/IDF1等指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) VLA-ReID：用“聚合的历史轨迹特征”作为查询，面向“当前帧所有检测”做全局匹配，训练时直接以视频级关联为目标，缩小训练-推理鸿沟。2) FCAE：从当前帧检测中估计“共同外观方向”。3) CAS：从轨迹与检测特征中移除该共同分量，抑制公共外观、凸显细微差异，无需额外标注。

Result: 在BEE24数据集上，相比SOTA跟踪器，HOTA +1.1，MOTA +0.3，AssR +2.6，AssA +0.7，IDF1 +0.8，并将ID切换减少28%。

Conclusion: 将re-ID重构为视频级全局关联训练，配合共同外观估计与抑制，可在高度相似与密集场景中显著降低ID切换并提升多项MOT指标，验证了视频级re-ID建模对外观关联的有效性。

Abstract: Multi-object tracking (MOT) aims to localize multiple objects in videos while preserving their identities over time. Long-term identity preservation remains difficult when objects are small, densely distributed, and highly similar in appearance, as in bee swarm scenes. Existing trackers rely on re-identification (re-ID) models trained through single-instance assignment (instance-level querying). At inference, however, MOT requires global assignment between multiple trajectories and detections, corresponding to video-level querying. This training-inference mismatch can cause identity switches among visually similar objects. Existing approaches also often require substantial additional annotations to enhance appearance discrimination. We propose Video-Level Association re-ID (VLA-ReID), which reformulates re-ID as video-level association modeling. It uses aggregated historical trajectory features as queries and all current-frame detections as candidates, enabling direct optimization of their global association at each frame. In addition, Frame-Common Appearance Estimation (FCAE) estimates a common appearance direction from current-frame detections, while Common-Appearance Suppression (CAS) removes the corresponding component along this direction from trajectory and detection features. This amplifies discriminative differences among highly similar objects without additional annotations. Experiments on BEE24 show that VLA-ReID improves HOTA by 1.1, MOTA by 0.3, AssR by 2.6, AssA by 0.7, and IDF1 by 0.8 over state-of-the-art trackers, while reducing identity switches by 28%. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of video-level re-ID modeling for appearance-based association in MOT.

### [108] [Cross-Coordinate Correspondence Pruning for Image-to-Point Cloud Registration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17200)
*Xin Liu,Rong Qin,Huipeng Lin,Leizhi Shu,Jin Wu,Chi-Man Vong,Liang Lin,Jufeng Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出跨坐标剪枝与多密度集合策略，缓解I2P配准中点云密度权衡，统一到图像坐标做轻量剪枝并跨密度合并去重，显著提升配准召回率（+8.6%以上）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无检测I2P配准采用粗到细，但忽视点云密度对粗对应质量与最终配准的决定性影响：过稀→内点不足，过密→外点比高，形成密度权衡，限制精度。

Method: 1) 跨坐标对应剪枝（CCP）：将粗匹配对投影到2D图像坐标以统一空间，利用轻量剪枝网络从几何坐标与模态特征两个维度预测内点置信度并滤除外点。2) 多密度点集合（MDPE）：在多种点云体素密度下分别生成并剪枝粗对应，然后融合与去重，以最大化内点召回。

Result: 在多基准上配准召回率相较SOTA至少提升8.6%，显示在不同密度设置下均获得更高质量的粗对应并提升最终配准。

Conclusion: 通过投影统一坐标、学习式剪枝与跨密度合并，突破点云密度权衡，获得更多且更纯净的内点，为I2P配准带来显著且稳定的性能提升。

Abstract: Recent detection-free approaches have shown significant efficacy in image-to-point cloud (I2P) registration by employing a coarse-to-fine matching pipeline. In the coarse stage, down-sampled image features and voxelized point cloud features are typically fused to establish initial coarse correspondences for subsequent refinement. However, existing methods largely overlook the critical role of point cloud density, which fundamentally dictates the quality of coarse correspondences and the final registration results. Specifically, excessively sparse point clouds lead to an insufficient number of inliers, while overly dense ones often introduce a high outlier ratio. Consequently, this creates an inherent density trade-off, thereby significantly limiting the registration accuracy of current approaches. For mitigating this trade-off, we propose a novel Cross-Coordinate Correspondences Pruning (CCP) strategy to acquire sufficient inliers while ensuring a low outlier ratio. To minimize interference from inter-modal coordinate discrepancies, we first project cross-coordinate coarse correspondences to the 2D image coordinate system for spatial unification. Subsequently, a lightweight pruning network is responsible for predicting the inlier confidences, which are used to filter coarse outliers, from coordinate geometric and modal feature dimensions. To maximize inlier recall, we further design a Multi-Density Point Ensemble (MDPE) strategy that consolidates and deduplicates pruned coarse correspondences across varying point cloud densities. Our method achieves a significant performance improvement, surpassing existing state-of-the-art methods by at least 8.6% in Registration Recall across various benchmarks.

Abstract: Automated polyp segmentation in colonoscopy continues to pose challenges due to substantial appearance variations and indistinct polyp boundaries. In addition, adopting multiple FMs together raises concerns, even though they encode complementary semantic and structural information. While lightweight models, including U-Net, PraNet and U-Net++, are computationally efficient, they often struggle to generalize across datasets due to limited representational capacity. To address this gap, we propose Lite-Polyp Inductor (Lite-Pi), a novel foundation model induction framework that significantly enhances lightweight polyp segmentation baselines. Our proposed framework generates FM-specific prototype representations and aligns them semantically with the corresponding foundation model priors through reconstruction-based supervision. Subsequently, transformer-based fusion is introduced to highlight the polyp relevant representations, including salient boundary information, while preserving complementary semantic cues. Extensive experiments across five polyp segmentation benchmark datasets demonstrate that Lite-π significantly improves lightweight baselines, achieving superior generalization performance with minimal computational overhead and thereby, offering a practical solution for generalized polyp segmentation. Our code is available at GitHub. https://github.com/lostinrepo/Lite-Pi

### [110] [Semantic Context Matters: Analysis of Color Names Across Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17221)
*Adilet Yerkin,Elnara Kadyrgali,Malika Ziyada,Nuray Toganas,Muragul Muratbekova,Ayan Igali,Aruzhan Sabitkyzy,Pakizar Shamoi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 研究表明，颜色命名受情境语义强烈影响：化妆品、蜡笔与车色在COLIBRI的86个模糊颜色范畴上分布显著不同。Crayola覆盖最广且最均衡，化妆品偏暖色，车色偏蓝与无彩。此框架有助于构建情境感知的颜色模型，改进设计分析、检索、推荐与人机系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统颜色命名多依赖数值色差或通用色词，却难以解释不同应用领域中对同一物理颜色的不同命名与理解。作者欲系统量化“情境（语义域）”对颜色命名分布的影响，并验证是否需要情境感知的颜色模型。

Method: 将三类真实世界色名数据集（化妆品、Crayola蜡笔、汽车颜色）映射到COLIBRI模型的86个模糊颜色范畴；以范畴覆盖率、香农熵（均衡度/多样性）与最大lift（情境-范畴的偏好强度）衡量情境差异；比较三情境在模糊色空间的占用与集中度。

Result: 覆盖率：化妆品48/86，Crayola 50/86，车色40/86；Crayola在空间上最广且最均衡；化妆品集中于暖色区域；车色在蓝色与无彩（黑白灰）区域更专门化；统计指标显示不同情境对特定范畴有显著偏好。

Conclusion: 颜色命名无法仅由数值相似性解释，语义情境是关键维度。提出的映射与度量框架可支持情境感知的颜色模型，服务于设计分析、产品搜索与推荐、人本AI等应用。

Abstract: Color naming is influenced not only by physical color values but also by the semantic context in which colors are used. This paper investigates context-dependent color naming by mapping color-name datasets from Cosmetics, Crayola, and Car-color vocabularies onto the 86 fuzzy color categories of the COLIBRI color model. Contextual variation is analyzed using category coverage, Shannon entropy, and maximum lift. The results show that the three contexts occupy the COLIBRI color space differently: Cosmetics covers 48 of 86 fuzzy categories, Crayola covers 50, and Car colors cover 40. The results demonstrated that Crayola provides the broadest and most balanced use of the fuzzy color space, Cosmetics is mainly concentrated around warm-tone regions, and Car colors are more specialized around blue and achromatic regions. These findings show that color naming cannot be fully explained by numerical color similarity alone and that semantic context plays an important role in human color interpretation. The proposed framework supports the development of context-aware color models for design analytics, product search, recommendation systems, and human-centered artificial intelligence.

</details>


### [111] [VecFontLLM: Anchor-Guided Direct Synthesis of Chinese Vector Fonts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17251)
*Hao Yuan,Yuxuan Luo,Xing Chen,Zhouhui Lian*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VecFontLLM：一种锚点引导的多模态大语言模型，分两阶段（锚架构→贝塞尔细化）直接少样本生成中文矢量字形，在复杂字上更稳定、高质，且无需栅格化与再矢量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中文矢量字形包含组件结构、锚点布局与贝塞尔细节等多尺度要素。传统将所有矢量命令串成长序列，导致长程依赖与复杂度高；直接矢量生成在复杂字失败率高，而栅格域方法需后续矢量化，损失结构与精度。需要一种既能直接在矢量域生成、又能稳健处理复杂汉字结构的少样本方法。

Method: 提出锚点引导的多模态LLM：1) 先预测并迭代细化锚点脚手架，确定组件与轮廓的粗布局；2) 在锚点基础上补全贝塞尔控制点，恢复局部曲率与风格；3) 测试时采用基于置信度的生成链，对组件候选进行采样并从最高置信度分支继续合成，提高复杂字稳定性。并在多个中文字体数据集上训练/评估。

Result: 实现首次高质量、少样本、直接在矢量域合成复杂中文字形；在矢量字体生成任务上显著优于现有直接矢量方法；渲染质量与栅格域基线具有竞争力；生成的矢量指令分布接近真实字体。

Conclusion: 锚点先行、分阶段的矢量生成范式有效缓解长序列与多尺度耦合难题，使复杂汉字的直接矢量合成成为可能；置信度引导的候选扩展提升了稳定性。方法为结构化矢量生成提供了通用思路。

Abstract: Direct generation of Chinese vector fonts is a challenging and ongoing problem. A Chinese vector glyph contains complex component structure, anchor layout, and Bézier curve details, which work at different scales, but a standard vector sequence writes them together in one long sequence, making the task of vector font synthesis challenging. Existing direct vector generators often fail on complex characters, while raster-domain methods must vectorize the synthesized glyph images afterward. To address the above-mentioned problem, this paper proposes VecFontLLM, an anchor-guided multimodal large language model for direct few-shot synthesis of Chinese vector fonts. Our key idea is to generate vector glyphs through anchors rather than a standard vector sequence. Specifically, the proposed VecFontLLM first predicts and refines an anchor scaffold that fixes the coarse layout of components and contours, and then completes Bézier control points to recover local curvature and style. At test time, a confidence-guided generation chain samples multiple component candidates and continues synthesis from the highest-confidence one, improving stability for complex glyphs. This work demonstrates, for the first time, high-quality few-shot synthesis of complex Chinese vector glyphs directly in the vector domain, without raster generation or vectorization. Experiments on several Chinese font datasets show substantial improvements over existing vector font synthesis methods, competitive glyph rendering quality against raster-domain baselines, and vector command distributions close to real fonts.

### [112] [PACE: Polar Axis-Conditioned Estimation for PairUAV Relative Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17268)
*Ze Rong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Polar Axis-Conditioned Estimation（PACE）：在共享的成对表征上，为极坐标的两个轴（航向与距离）提供独立的读出接口，分别利用不同深度与路径的证据，从而缓解将两者当作同质坐标联合解码带来的耦合与误配问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PairUAV相对定位将航向与距离作为同质输出，由同一解码器证据与优化状态驱动。这导致：两轴偏好不同的解码深度组合却被迫共享；在验证轨迹上最佳检查点常不一致（80.8%不一致）；距离误差分布有显著高尾。作者希望在保留共享成对表示的同时，打破读出阶段的耦合，使各轴利用最有利的证据路径。

Method: 维持Reloc3r风格的共享成对图像表示；在读出阶段进行轴条件化：为航向与距离分别配置接口。航向读出侧重中/后期的关系证据（relational evidence）；距离读出走直接的后期度量路径（metric path）。通过受控读出探针分析各层证据贡献并据此设计架构。

Result: 在官方隐藏测试上：最强公开原始预测器得分0.002460；互补的PAAER预测器得分0.002514且角度误差略低；采用确定性的挑战打包（与学习估计分开报告）后，最终成绩0.001874。另报告航向/距离最佳检查点在验证轨迹上80.8%不一致，距离误差出现独特高误差尾。

Conclusion: 将极坐标两轴解耦到轴特定读出，在共享表示上实现差异化证据利用，可缓解优化耦合与误配，提升总体成绩与角度估计稳定性。提供代码、权重、预测与重建工具以复现与扩展。

Abstract: PairUAV relative localization maps two UAV images to a polar navigation command. Although heading and range share the same pairwise pose context, treating them as homogeneous coordinates forces both outputs to use the same decoder evidence and optimization state. Controlled readout probes reveal a different structure: the two axes favor different decoder-depth combinations, their best checkpoints disagree on 80.8% of a validation trajectory, and range errors exhibit a distinct high-error tail. We introduce method, Polar Axis-Conditioned Estimation, which retains a shared Reloc3r-style pair representation while assigning axis-specific readout interfaces. Heading uses mid/late relational evidence, whereas range remains attached to a direct late metric path. On the official hidden test, the strongest released raw predictor scores 0.002460; the complementary PAAER predictor scores 0.002514 with a slightly lower angle error. Deterministic challenge packaging, reported separately from learned estimation, yields the final score of 0.001874. Code, checkpoints, predictions, and reconstruction tools are available at https://github.com/zerong7777-boop/PairUAV-PACE.

### [113] [MIS-HCC: Hierarchical Channel Clustering for Efficient Medical Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17329)
*Bo Zhao,Haoran Yu,Lifei Liu,Zongcheng Chu,Yining Liu,Chang Liu,Szu-Yu Chen,Zequn Xie*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MIS-HCC：用层内通道的层次聚类与参数融合，实现医学图像分割模型在轻量化同时保持精度。以Wasserstein距离度量通道相似性，指导聚类与融合；在三数据集上优于SOTA的精度与压缩率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学分割模型需高精度且能在资源受限平台部署；现有剪枝多忽视网络内部结构间的内在联系与相似性，压缩后难以保留预训练基础特征。

Method: 对预训练模型各层通道计算分布相似度（Wasserstein距离）形成相似度矩阵；执行层次聚类，将同簇通道进行参数融合（而非简单剪除），得到更小的网络。整体流程：通道相似度度量→层次聚类→通道融合→得到压缩模型并微调。

Result: 在三个医学影像数据集上，MIS-HCC在分割精度与压缩效率上均优于现有方法（SOTA），表明在减少计算与参数的同时维持或提升性能。

Conclusion: 利用层次聚类与Wasserstein距离驱动的通道融合能在不显著牺牲（甚至提升）分割性能的前提下大幅压缩模型，为资源受限医疗平台部署提供可行方案。

Abstract: Medical image segmentation models require both high accuracy and lightweight design to accommodate real-world medical applications. The deployment of these models on resource-limited medical platforms remains a significant challenge due to their high computational and parameter requirements. Existing pruning methods for model compression mostly overlook the intrinsic connections and similarity between the internal structures of complex deep neural networks. As a result, compressed models may not effectively retain the basic features of the pretrained network. To solve this problem, we propose a hierarchical clustering compression method for medical image segmentation models (MIS-HCC). This approach employs hierarchical clustering to partition channels and fuse their parameters efficiently. Specifically, it leverages the Wasserstein distance to represent similarity of channels within layers of pre-trained network, forming a similarity matrix that guides the clustering process. Channels within each cluster are then fused to produce a compressed network. Experimental results on three medical image datasets application demonstrate that MIS-HCC outperforms the state-of-the-art methods in both accuracy and compression efficiency, offering an effective solution for deploying medical image segmentation models on resource-limited medical platforms.

### [114] [Orthogonal Knowledge Refreshing for Domain-Incremental Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17340)
*Aoting Zhang,Dongbao Yang,Chang Liu,Xiaopeng Hong,Can Ma,Yu Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出OKR用于领域增量目标检测，通过为每个领域建立低秩分支子空间并在融合时用正交梯度刷新与拓扑一致性约束，达到无忘却的持续适应，显著提升mAP。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DIOD需在不断引入新领域时保持旧知识，但参数高效微调虽节省参数，却易引发跨领域干扰与遗忘，导致性能下降，需一种既能扩展容量又避免干扰的方案。

Method: - 结构：在冻结预训练模型的基础上，为每个领域增添专属的低秩适配分支，形成独立域特定子空间；推理时无域选择，融合各子空间实现整体判别。
- 正交刷新：基于梯度的投影策略，将新领域的梯度更新投影到历史融合子空间的正交补上，减少对已学知识的干扰。
- 拓扑一致性：引入拓扑感知一致性约束，使新旧领域的语义结构对齐，缓解语义碎片化。
- 训练范式：逐域增量训练，每域仅更新其低秩分支参数与与之相关的融合/投影模块。

Result: 在Pascal VOC与BDD100K系列上，相较当前最优的无样本（exemplar-free）方法，mAP分别提升+5.6%与+6.5%，验证了方法的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: OKR通过域特定低秩子空间的无冲突扩容、正交梯度刷新与拓扑一致性对齐，实现了在DIOD中的持续适应与抗遗忘，并在标准基准上取得显著增益。

Abstract: Domain-incremental object detection (DIOD) requires models to continually adapt to new domains while preserving prior knowledge. Recently, parameter-efficient fine-tuning offers a promising avenue, wherein a pre-trained model is frozen and a small number of learnable parameters are injected for downstream tasks. However, these methods risk overwriting critical past knowledge, triggering inter-domain interference and performance degradation. To address this challenge, we propose Orthogonal Knowledge Refreshing (OKR), a simple yet effective framework for DIOD. OKR incrementally constructs independent domain-specific subspaces via dedicated low-rank branches for each domain, which are seamlessly fused for a holistic decision, enabling conflict-free capacity expansion without domain selection during inference. To minimize knowledge interference during fusion, we present a gradient-based orthogonal refreshing strategy that projects gradient updates of new domains onto the orthogonal complement of the fused historical subspace, supporting continual adaptation without forgetting. Moreover, to mitigate semantic fragmentation across domains, we enforce topology-aware consistency, aligning the semantic structures of old and new domains. Extensive experiments validate the superiority of OKR, outperforming the best exemplar-free method by significant margins of +5.6% and +6.5% mAP on the Pascal VOC and BDD100K series, respectively.

</details>


### [115] [Understanding From Human Perspective: A Multi-agent System for Interactive Egocentric Medical Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17341)
*Rongjun Ge,Dongyang Wang,Heng Zhu,Zhirui Li,Yang Chen,Yuting He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出EgoMed-Agent，一个面向智能眼镜的交互式第一视角医学图像分割系统，通过目标确认与定位引导传播两条工作流，分别解决语义歧义与视觉变化问题，在平均Dice上达71.34%，显著超越文本提示基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IEMIS可为临床复核提供目标级证据，但第一视角带来两大难题：用户指令语义不确定，导致无法确定真正目标；相机运动与场景变化使分割在视频帧间漂移，影响稳定性与可靠性。

Method: 构建多智能体系统EgoMed-Agent：1) 目标确认工作流：将用户指令与候选目标进行语义落地并打可靠性分，可靠时确认目标，不可靠时交互询问澄清；2) 定位引导的传播工作流：将逐帧目标定位与掩膜传播耦合，当定位与传播出现偏差时用定位结果校正传播掩膜，保证跨帧一致性。

Result: 在广泛实验中，EgoMed-Agent取得平均Dice 71.34%，远高于最佳文本提示基线11.70%。

Conclusion: 通过“先确认后传播、传播中用定位纠偏”的双工作流，多智能体EgoMed-Agent有效缓解第一视角下的语义歧义与视觉漂移，实现稳定准确的交互式医学目标分割，并显著优于现有基线。

Abstract: Interactive egocentric medical image segmentation (IEMIS) plays an important role in smart-glasses-assisted medical image review, segmenting the medical targets a clinician refers to from their egocentric view. Once it succeeds, the object-level visual evidence it provides strengthens the review and underpins fine-grained analysis and clinical decision-making. However, the instruction and the video both come from the user's egocentric perspective, which poses two challenges. (1) Semantic ambiguity leaves the model unable to confirm the user-intended target. (2) Visual variability makes the segmentation jump from frame to frame. In this paper, we propose EgoMed-Agent, a multi-agent system that understands the target from the human perspective through two workflows. (1) The \textit{Target Confirmation Workflow} grounds the instruction against candidate targets with a reliability score, confirming the target when the grounding is reliable and asking the user to clarify when it is not, thereby confirming the segmentation target. (2) The \textit{Localization-Guided Propagation Workflow} couples mask propagation with per-frame target localization, using the localized target to correct the propagated mask whenever the two diverge, so the segmentation stays on the target across the egocentric video. Extensive experiments show that EgoMed-Agent reaches 71.34\% average Dice, far above the best text-prompted baseline (11.70\%). Our code is available at \href{https://github.com/wdyyyyyy/EgoMed-Agent}{our project page}.

### [116] [STAR: Skeletal Token Alignment and Rearrangement for Interaction Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17342)
*Yuhang Wen,Mengyuan Liu,Zixuan Tang,Junsong Yuan,Sirui Li,Beichen Ding*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出STAR方法，通过对齐骨架与RGB表征，在仅骨架推理下也能利用视觉线索，显著提升人-机/人-人交互识别表现。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出STAR（Skeletal Token Alignment and Rearrangement）：1）骨架编码器：通过实体重排（ER）与交互式时空Token（ISTs）建模细粒度关联系统；2）视觉交互编码：引入FoI（专注交互）策略，在RGB视频中聚焦与交互相关的时空区域；3）跨模态对齐：采用对比学习在共享潜空间对齐骨架与RGB表征，并用精炼头进一步提升预测。训练期使用骨架+RGB，推理期仅用骨架。

Result: 在Chico、HARPER、NTU Mutual 11与26等数据集上，较现有方法取得一致的SOTA性能提升（具体数值未在摘要给出）。

Abstract: Understanding physical human-robot and human-human interactions is a challenging yet emerging topic in 3D vision. While most existing methods rely on skeleton sequences--effective in low-light and privacy-sensitive environment--they face two major challenges: 1) learning and effectively exploiting interaction cues from skeletal data, and 2) compensating for the lack of visual information absent in skeletons alone. To address these challenges, we propose skeletal token alignment and rearrangement (STAR) for human-robot and human-human interaction recognition. It learns interaction-specific skeleton features and enriches them using visual cues by aligning skeleton and RGB video representations in a shared latent space. Specifically, STAR consists of three key components. First, we design a skeleton encoder that captures fine-grained interdependencies using Entity Rearrangement (ER) and Interactive Spatiotemporal Tokens (ISTs). Second, we present Visual Interaction Encoding that introduces a Focus on Interactions (FoI) strategy to attend to spatiotemporal regions relevant to interactions in RGB videos. Finally, these representations are aligned via a contrastive learning objective, with a refinement head further refines predictions. During training, STAR leverages both skeleton and RGB video data to learn robust, discriminative interaction representations. At inference time, it operates on skeletons alone, retaining visual-informed benefits while preserving skeleton-only efficiency. Extensive experiments on Chico, HARPER, NTU Mutual 11 and 26 datasets consistently validate our approach by demonstrating superior performance over state-of-the-art methods. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/Necolizer/STAR.

### [117] [SkyVLaM: Multimodal Large Language Model for UAV Video Understanding in Remote Sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17386)
*Kaiwen Jing,Ruixu Jia,Bingyao Li,Ruizhe Ou,Ming Wu,Chuang Zhang*

TL;DR: 提出SkyVLaM用于无人机视频的语言条件分割，结合稀疏/致密时空token与LLM，实现更高效token预算与更优分割；并发布含标注的数据集SkyVid。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UAV视频中目标小、模糊且视角动态，现有MLLM在语言条件分割上受限于视觉token预算与时序建模不足，需要更高效的时空表示与细粒度对齐能力。

Method: 1) 以Temporal Basis Perceiver从视频patch表征中直接构建稀疏时序基token；2) 对稀疏基施加正则以鼓励互补时序线索；3) 自适应选择时间一致的致密高分辨片段进行精细检查；4) 将稀疏+致密token联合输入LLM，实现查询条件分割。另构建SkyVid数据集，含SkyVid-VGCG与SkyVid-RVOS两个子集与像素级标注。

Result: 在UAV场景的语言条件视频分割任务上，SkyVLaM更高效地分配视觉token预算并取得优于现有方法的性能；数据集规模为101段视频、3.36万帧、153万像素级目标实例。

Conclusion: 稀疏-致密协同的时空token与LLM融合可显著提升UAV视频的语言条件分割效果；SkyVid为相关研究提供了基准与数据支撑。

Abstract: Recent advances in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have significantly improved remote sensing (RS) multimodal understanding. Language-conditioned segmentation is crucial for fine-grained target understanding in Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) videos. However, this task remains challenging due to the prevalence of small, visually ambiguous targets and dynamic aerial perspectives. In this paper, we propose SkyVLaM, a multimodal large language model for UAV video understanding. SkyVLaM constructs sparse tokens directly from patch-level video representations through a temporal basis perceiver, regularizes the sparse basis to encourage complementary temporal cues, and adaptively selects a temporally coherent dense segment for high-resolution inspection. The resulting sparse and dense tokens are jointly processed by a large language model for query-conditioned segmentation. We further build SkyVid, consisting of SkyVid-VGCG and SkyVid-RVOS for video grounded conversation generation and referring video object segmentation, respectively. SkyVid contains 101 videos, 33.6K frames, and 1.53M pixel-level object instances. Experiments show that SkyVLaM provides a more effective allocation of the visual token budget and improves language-conditioned video segmentation in UAV scenarios.

### [118] [Automating Visual Recognition of Leprosy in Wild Chimpanzees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17395)

Abstract: Leprosy (Mycobacterium leprae) has been confirmed in wild western chimpanzees (Pan troglodytes verus) in West Africa, presenting as clear and progressive visual symptoms. We benchmark spatial (2D), temporally aggregated (2.5D), and video-based (3D) classification approaches to investigate which approach is best suited to automated leprosy detection in wild apes. We find that simple aggregation of crop-level predictions consistently matches or outperforms both learned temporal models and end-to-end video architectures -- consistent with leprosy's static cutaneous presentation. We further find that performance is suppressed when tracklets contain frames of partially visible individuals -- as commonly occurs at the start and end of a track -- and demonstrate that this can be addressed through targeted construction and aggregation strategies.

### [120] [Does Super-Resolution Preserve Defect Evidence? A Low-False-Call Benchmark for Semiconductor Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17401)
*Shaoliang Yang,Jun Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出一个基准来评估超分辨在晶圆/缺陷检测中的“看起来更清晰但丢失证据”的失败模式，发现高重建相似度并不等于更好的缺陷检测与可迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业检测常用超分辨提升图像清晰度，但可能破坏检测所需的微弱证据；现有评估多以重建质量（如SSIM）为主，忽略在固定低误报操作点下的检测可用性与跨分布（形态/纹理）迁移。

Method: 构建一个把重建与检测解耦的基准：合成线/空与接触孔图像，进行10次独立重复；包含模型训练、独立校准、干净对照、弱缺陷与一种保留未见过的缺陷形态。使用统一的局部残差检测器对所有重建进行打分；另设直接检测与联合训练两条比较轨。固定在预声明的低误报率下评估召回与可行性（是否满足持出限制），并将同一策略外推到Carinthia-S真实SEM纹理上。

Result: 两种学习型重建模型虽取得最高SSIM，但在每一次配对重复中，缺陷像素召回都低于双三次插值，显示“高保真重建≠更好检测”。直接检测器DeepLabV3在FPR≈1.74e-4下达到召回约0.1984±0.0385，且10/10次满足持出可行性。示例联合模型DPU-WaferSR在独立干净校准集上合格，但在持出设置中10/10次超限，说明校准成功不保证迁移。对弱缺陷，所有可行方法召回近零。将相同策略用于4591个Carinthia-S掩膜时，出现显著与方法相关的分布漂移。

Conclusion: 评估用于检测的超分辨时，应以“保留任务证据”和“操作点可迁移性”作为核心指标，而非仅以重建质量（如SSIM）判断；直接检测可能优于联合/重建先行方案，且需要在低误报约束和跨分布条件下检验。

Abstract: Super-resolution can make inspection images appear sharper without preserving the evidence needed to detect a defect. We study this failure mode with a benchmark that separates reconstruction from detection and evaluates both at a predeclared low false-positive rate. Ten end-to-end repetitions combine independently generated line/space and contact-hole images with model training, calibration, clean controls, weak defects, and a held-out defect morphology. Every reconstruction is scored by the same local residual detector, while direct and jointly trained detectors form a separate comparison track. Reconstruction fidelity and inspection utility diverge: the two learned reconstruction models attain the highest structural similarity yet detect fewer defect pixels than bicubic interpolation in every paired repetition. A direct DeepLabV3 detector reaches $0.1984\pm0.0385$ recall at $0.000174\pm0.000084$ false-positive rate and satisfies the held-out feasibility criterion in all ten repetitions. An illustrative joint model, DPU-WaferSR, passes independent clean calibration but exceeds the held-out limit in all ten repetitions, demonstrating that calibration success does not guarantee transfer. Weak-defect recall remains near zero for every feasible method. Applying the unchanged policies to 4,591 public Carinthia-S masks further reveals large method-dependent shifts on real SEM texture. These results support a simple conclusion: super-resolution for inspection should be judged by preserved task evidence and operating-point transfer, not reconstruction quality alone.

*Yuhan Zhu,Changlian Ma,Xiangyu Zeng,Xinhao Li,Zhiqiu Zhang,Songze Li,Jun Zhang,Tianxiang Jiang,Yuandong Yang,Ziang Yan,Zikang Wang,Xinyu Chen,Haoran Chen,Shaowei Zhang,Limin Wang*

TL;DR: TimeLens2 将视频证据看作“时间区间集合”来训练与评估，提出可靠多段监督数据构建与匹配无关的最优传输型奖励，统一解决不同长度、域与查询形式下的通用视频时间定位，并在多基准上显著超越同规模与更大开源模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 视证据为时间区间集合，贯穿监督与优化；2) 数据：TimeLens2-93K，通过字幕生成候选、多代理独立定位、共识聚合、语义验证与边界细化，得到可靠多段标注；3) 训练奖励：提出时间Wasserstein（精确计算一维W1，基于并集支撑的均匀分布），在基数不等与等效碎片化时提供稠密、无需匹配的反馈；辅以tIoU奖励提供精确重叠信号；4) 模型扩展至2B/4B/8B规模。

Result: 在7个基准上，TimeLens2-2B全面优于同规模基线；4B与8B达SOTA，甚至超过参数高达397B的开源模型。相较各自Qwen3-VL骨干，2B/4B/8B分别提升mIoU 14.2/13.0/18.1点。

Conclusion: 以区间集合为核心表示，并结合稳健的数据构建与Wasserstein+tIoU奖励，可统一而有效地解决通用视频时间定位，在多基准上取得显著与可扩展的性能优势。

Abstract: Video multimodal large language models (MLLMs) can describe what happens in a video, but rarely identify when the supporting evidence occurs. We study generalist video temporal grounding, in which one model predicts a variable-cardinality set of evidence intervals across video lengths, domains, query forms, and viewpoints. Existing training strategies are misaligned with this set-valued task: long-video labels often rely on brittle one-pass annotation, while reinforcement-learning rewards either fail to distinguish non-overlapping predictions or require fragile segment matching. TimeLens2 treats temporal evidence as an interval set throughout supervision and optimization. TimeLens2-93K constructs reliable multi-span supervision through caption-derived proposals, independent localization, cross-agent consensus, semantic verification, and boundary refinement. Our temporal Wasserstein reward computes exact one-dimensional \(W_1\) between uniform distributions over merged interval supports, providing dense, matching-free feedback under unequal cardinalities and equivalent fragmentation; temporal IoU complements it with precise-overlap feedback. Across seven benchmarks, TimeLens2-2B outperforms all size-matched baselines on every benchmark, while the 4B and 8B variants achieve state-of-the-art performance, surpassing open-source models with up to 397B parameters. The 2B, 4B, and 8B variants improve over their Qwen3-VL backbones by 14.2, 13.0, and 18.1 mIoU points, respectively.

### [122] [An Explainable FFT-Based Spatial-Frequency Fusion Framework for Deepfake Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17441)
*Pamela Kirui,Cho Hyuk,Qingzhong Liu,Haodi Jiang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深伪导致真实性与信任危机；现有空域或频域单独使用受限，且主流DCT管线常需频-像逆变换、复杂度高且信息可能受损；需要一种高效、互补、可解释的空频融合检测框架。

Method: 构建双分支：1) 空域：部分微调的Xception提取空间特征；2) 频域：对图像做FFT，取对数量级谱幅值，经浅层卷积提特征，无需逆变换。两分支特征分别经Transformer编码器细化，再通过多尺度交叉注意力进行融合，最后经MLP完成真伪分类。提供Grad-CAM/LIME与频谱解析以提升可解释性。

Result: 在与最先进的DCT型空频融合方法及多种基线的比较中，MSCA-FFT在多项实验中取得持续更高的检测性能；消融显示频域分支与空域互补，融合后性能显著提升。

Conclusion: FFT频域分支能在不做逆变换的前提下提供关键光谱线索；与空域通过交叉注意力融合可更稳健地区分真伪；模型在眼、口、鼻及人脸边界等操控敏感区域表现出一致的可解释关注，证明方法有效且具可解释性。

Abstract: Deepfake generation has raised growing concerns regarding digital media authenticity, misinformation, identity fraud, and public trust. Recent studies show that combining spatial and frequency features leads to stronger detection results than using independently. This paper presents MSCA-FFT, a Fast Fourier Transform (FFT)-based multi-scale cross-attention framework for image-level deepfake detection. The model combines a partially fine-tuned Xception spatial branch with an FFT-based frequency branch. The frequency branch processes the log-scaled FFT magnitude spectrum through shallow convolutional layers, avoiding inverse frequency-to-image reconstruction used in DCT-based pipelines. The spatial and frequency representations are refined by transformer encoders, fused through cross-attention, and passed to an MLP classifier for real/fake prediction. Experimental results show that MSCA-FFT achieves consistently higher performance than the DCT-based state-of-the-art spatial-frequency fusion method and the compared baseline models. The ablation study further indicates that the FFT-based frequency branch provides complementary spectral cues when fused with spatial features. In addition, FFT-based frequency analysis and Grad-CAM/LIME explanations show consistent evidence around manipulation-sensitive facial regions, including the eyes, mouth, nose, and facial boundaries.
